European Correspondence

After the Signing of the German-Japanese Pact 27

— Lieshan

The Germans are Familiar with Japan

The sensational "German-Japanese Anti-Comintern Pact" has been signed for two weeks now. In these short two weeks, the Japanese have undoubtedly been considered the happiest race in the world. Because from the moment the treaty was announced, a portion of Germans suddenly discovered a new race, a new ambition, and a country as worthy of human respect as Germany. The joy of the Germans, especially the joy of the Japanese, is everywhere filled with pleasant air. If you meet a young member of the National Socialist Party, even if he knows you are Chinese, this kind of joy cannot be restrained from showing itself. He will tell you the significance of this pact in world history, and at the same time, he will especially remind you of how excellent the Japanese race is. Finally, he concludes that within a few years, the world's leading countries will be subject to "natural" elimination. His eyes glowed as if predicting that "a new era has been born!" This frank statement is considered a sign of German honesty! However, you are Chinese, you know the relationship between China and Japan, you know that the German business community values ​​China's friendship, and you also know that even if Germany and Japan really form a military alliance, Germany will not have much military power to send to the Far East to help Japan deal with China. You tell him all this, you remind him not to repeat the mistakes of the European war. He thinks for a moment and says; maybe the Japanese will use Germany, but who knows if Germany is not using Japan? Well, the Chinese nation, China's friendship is naturally worthless in his eyes. This is the international political concept of the youth of the "Third Reich". We admire the courage of the Germans, but we still cannot find the need for Germany to offend China. Currently, China is a unified country. The dream of treating China as a colony, even the British "die-hards" have changed their views, let alone other European countries! German-Chinese trade has surged in the past year, and we believe that Germany is not short of wise men who will consider their own economic interests.

In fact, only some people in Germany welcome this pact, at least not all Germans. Everyone has not forgotten the lessons learned during the European war. Although the efforts of this group to propagandize are already astonishing. It is said that the pro-Japanese sentiment in Berlin's social circles is more Japanese than the Japanese themselves. They spread this concept to the people: first, Japan is anti-Russian and anti-communist, with the same fate as Germany. Secondly, the Japanese are also an excellent race in the world. But most importantly, the general German believes that in the event of a war between Germany and Russia, they can get the strength of Japan to help. So in the winter of 1936, the Japanese suddenly became the "comrades" of the Germans, or even more. Japan fever is a social phenomenon this year. Even when girls encounter yellow-faced foreigners on the road, they no longer say "Japanese devils" (Jabst). They will say in a sympathetic tone, in a sympathetic tone peculiar to girls: "Ah! That's a Japanese!"

Because the current pro-Japanese phenomenon is top-down, the German political party authorities have been particularly busy for the past two weeks. For example, German leader Adolf Hitler, in addition to hosting a banquet for Japanese Embassy personnel in Germany to celebrate the success of the pact, also specially issued a congratulatory telegram for the 10th anniversary of the founding of the Japanese Academy in Berlin. Another example is Mr. Ribbentrop, the German Ambassador to the United Kingdom. He traveled back and forth between London and Berlin, and I don’t know how much effort he spent just to sign this pact. His honorable appearance can be seen everywhere in news films recently. In addition, he also issued a statement proving the value of this pact. Another example is Mr. Rosenberg, the Minister of the Foreign Political Department of the National Socialist Party. He is currently a key figure in charge of German foreign policy. The Japanese Domei News Agency even spared no expense to conduct a "visit record" with him on wireless telephone from distant Tokyo. Of course, the busiest person is Dr. Goebbels, the Minister of Propaganda of Germany. He not only plans the overall propaganda affairs, but also wants to give public speeches to the people. In particular, under his guidance, German newspapers have a consistent line to promote German-Japanese friendship.

The Japanese are an excellent race, and Mr. Hitler also has this view. After the closing of the World Games, he told a reporter that when he - Mr. Hitler, saw the posture of the Japanese marathon winner running, he could not help but think of this admirable Japanese race. However, Mr. Hitler's example is a bit inappropriate. He did not find out the relationship between the winner and the Japanese race beforehand, so he got the premise wrong. Because the winner is not the "excellent" Japanese, but precisely the Korean who is oppressed by the "excellent" kind.

The Germans say that the Japanese are an excellent race. What do the Japanese say in this atmosphere? Taking advantage of the 10th anniversary of the founding of the Japanese Academy, a Japanese professor gave a speech on "The Origin of the Japanese". He does not admit that the Japanese are a mixed race of Mongolians, Malays, Koreans, etc. The reason, according to the research of modern Japanese linguists, is that Japanese is an independent writing. A kind of writing cannot be found in other countries in the world. Therefore, the Japanese are a special race, which is the conclusion of this professor.

It is said that the arguments in the newspapers represent public opinion, which is the so-called public opinion. Therefore, if we want to observe the phenomenon of German-Japanese friendship, we naturally have to look for materials in the German newspapers, especially the National Socialist Party newspapers. Summarizing the arguments of this group of newspapers, we can get a formula, that is: Japan is a country with an "ancient" culture, Japan is a military power, Japan is a vanguard against communism and Russia, the Japanese are as excellent as the Germans... and so on. Some people are also worried about this group of reporters, fearing that such praising materials will be finished soon. However, people who are familiar with the situation of the German press cannot help but sympathize with this group of reporters, naturally not only because of the relationship of "colleagues".

In fact, what does it have to do with us Chinese if people are anti-communist, anti-Russian, and pro-Japanese! If people do not hinder the interests of China, we have no reason to be jealous. But is this actually the case! According to the statement made by the German Ambassador to the Chinese government, the German-Japanese Pact will definitely not hinder the interests of China and the friendship between China and Germany. Naturally, this is not only our hope, but we can even understand the sincerity of the German government. However, judging from the arguments in the German newspapers about the recent Sino-Japanese events and the posted telegrams, there is at least no way to eliminate our doubts.

In the past two weeks, almost all of the Far East telegrams published by German newspapers have been exclusively handled by the semi-official German News Agency. Nine-tenths of the sources of the telegrams came from Tokyo, and only one-tenth came from the agency's resident reporters in China. The content of the telegrams from Tokyo is almost the same as that of the Japanese Domei News Agency. Not only does it quote Japan's position on factual matters, but also the wording is the same. For example, when describing the recent negotiations between the Japanese Ambassador to China and Foreign Minister Zhang, the agency calls the Japanese Ambassador "Ambassador" and calls Foreign Minister Zhang simply "Zhang". The status of a Minister of Foreign Affairs is not as good as that of an ambassador. The politeness of the agency's resident reporters seems to be not normal. What is especially puzzling is that the agency's telegrams often intentionally or unintentionally plead for Japan, as if Japan's actions were the result of China's coercion. We once sympathized with Germany after the European War when it was oppressed by others. Unexpectedly, on this day, it is not willing to give a fair criticism to our current struggles, a nation's struggle for survival! The big reason is that the Chinese government does not yet have a kind of news policy, so people can not bother to consider these things, naturally! What is even more bizarre about these telegrams is the arguments of the newspapers. For example, the "National Observer", the organ of the National Socialist Party, recently published an article quoting Sir Lytton's report to the League of Nations in 1932, saying that the Chinese Communist Party is very powerful and has a population of about 90 million. The implication seems to be that China will always be red too early, and the only way to save the Far East is to let Japan rule China. This reporter has been stationed in China for many years and is very clear about the current situation in China and the power of the Communist Party. Why ignore conscience, obliterate facts and agree with the Japanese? Is it because of the German-Japanese alliance that it is necessary to fabricate some rumors for China? Opposing Soviet Russia and opposing the Communist Party is none of our business. But when China is insulted, the Chinese people cannot sit idly by.

Another National Socialist Party newspaper even said in an editorial that we Chinese should not oppose Japan. The reason is that Soviet Russia occupied China's Outer Mongolia and Xinjiang, and China did not speak; Japan occupied the three northeastern provinces and Jehol, and China resisted desperately. It seems that China is not fair to Japan and Russia. This kind of argument that interferes in other countries' internal affairs may be pleasing to the Japanese. But at the same time, they must also remember that this is precisely an insult to China.

Recently, there have been many rumors that Germany will follow Italy in recognizing the puppet state of Manchuria, the question is only whether Japan can come up with appropriate exchange conditions. This is not only an opportunity for the German government to prove the friendship between China and Germany, but also in our Chinese eyes, it is very important to us, at least it will make us clear where we are standing! (December 10)

Tokyo Correspondence

1937 Annual Review of Japanese Finance (4) 39

— Nan Ling

If what the Minister of Finance says isn't mere official rhetoric, then it's overly optimistic. Looking at the current international situation, defense spending can only expand year by year. Not only military expenditures for the army and navy, but also industrial promotion fees and national livelihood stabilization fees, which are considered broad defense expenditures, will inevitably continue to increase. If there are no tax increases or new bond issuances, where will these inevitably expanding expenses be sourced?

Currently, Japan, in all aspects, is moving towards greater control. Many Japanese people, in conversation, even mockingly refer to it as the "era of control." The result of this control will be the decline of some industries and the sudden flourishing of others. Achieving genuine economic prosperity for society will be difficult. Even if prosperity is achieved, leading to natural revenue increases, the resulting tax increases and rising prices will inevitably lead to increased expenditures. Therefore, the optimistic tone of the financial authorities is, in reality, simply because they have already placed unprecedented pressure on the masses and cannot help but promise them a beautiful future. What is the actual state of Japanese finance? It is one where the burden on the masses will not be alleviated year after year.

According to the Japanese Ministry of Commerce and Industry's 1937 trade outlook: It is believed that Japan's trade in 1937 will be better than in 1936. With the establishment of a massive budget as its foundation, the military supply industry will surely flourish. Rice and silkworm cocoons, the two mainstays of rural areas, will also see increased sales as a result. At the same time, general small and medium-sized commercial and industrial enterprises will also prosper due to the activity of the military supply industry. Therefore, Japan's finances in 1937 are very optimistic.

Perhaps this can become a reality? But it is only a cosmeticized fact. Moreover, to realize this cosmeticized fact, it is necessary to implement drastic control and strengthening measures.

First, strengthen trade controls. The "Imperial Economic Conference," currently underway, linking Japan, Manchuria, Korea, and North China, is discussing how to prevent the deterioration of trade next year. The so-called "Manchukuo Industrial Five-Year Plan" and "North China Economic Development" are both establishing the foundation for a quasi-wartime economic system. The current world is moving towards the end of capitalism. The lively progression of capitalism is impossible to develop as desired. To make it flourish and adapt to a quasi-wartime tax system, it is essential to implement strengthened trade controls.

Second, strengthen capital controls. After issuing more public bonds, the Ministry of Finance will inevitably adopt a more enhanced policy on exchange rate management to prevent capital flight. On the one hand, strengthen the low-interest rate policy in line with the trade control policy to control financial capital. Use administrative means to shift the public bond digestion method from a natural digestion method to an artificial digestion method to establish the foundation of the public bond national policy.

Third, strengthen industrial controls. Centering on the military supply industry, implement various industrial controls from various perspectives. Impose strict controls on various industrial forms of export and import, as well as raw materials and profits, to create a crippled economy that can adapt to the prosperity of the military supply industry.

Due to the strengthening of these control policies, Japanese finance in 1937 will naturally appear in a new form. This new form is:

One hand presses down on the masses, while the other hand raises the banner of enriching national defense and developing industry. (December 14)

Current Commentary

On the Eve of the Expiration of Naval Treaties 40

— Li

In two days, the Washington and London Naval Treaties concluded by the five countries of Great Britain, the United States, Japan, France, and Italy will expire. We know that these two treaties were relatively successful arms limitation treaties after the Great War. The former was established in 1922. In addition to limiting the tonnage of battleships of the signatory countries, it also maintained the balance of power between Great Britain, the United States, and Japan in the Pacific. The latter was established in 1930 and limited the tonnage of auxiliary ships of the signatory countries. For more than ten years, the signatory countries have still been actively expanding their armaments and engaging in maritime rivalry, but they have always been constrained by the treaties and have been unable to avoid certain restrictions. Now that these two treaties are about to expire and become ineffective, the naval powers will naturally actively prepare to expand their armaments again without restriction and launch a maritime arms race.

Before the expiration of the naval treaties, the five countries of Great Britain, the United States, France, Japan, and Italy had engaged in tortuous negotiations on ways to limit armaments after the expiration of the naval treaties. However, due to the conflicting interests of the participating countries, only the Anglo-American-French Agreement was produced. This agreement, because it did not include countries such as Japan and Italy, cannot be equated with the Washington and London Naval Treaties in terms of its effect. Moreover, the agreement further stipulated that if countries other than the signatory countries actively expand their armaments beyond the appropriate ratio stipulated by the Washington Naval Treaty, the signatory countries may also lift their treaty obligations and engage in free competition. This provision, at a time when Japan and Italy are about to lift their treaty obligations and actively expand their armaments, is tantamount to opening a convenient door for arms expansion. Secondly, although Great Britain has also concluded naval agreements with Germany and the Soviet Union, stipulating the ratio of the naval power of the two countries to that of Great Britain, the naval power that Great Britain has allowed Germany to retain has not yet been fully accepted by France, and Great Britain has also allowed the Soviet Union to freely build a Far Eastern navy on the condition that Japan does not join the Tripartite Agreement. This kind of infighting diplomacy not only cannot limit the competition for armaments, but also is enough to promote the rate of arms expansion.

Sure enough, after the establishment of the Tripartite Agreement, Great Britain immediately announced the reservation of 40,000 tons of destroyers whose ship age had exceeded the limit. Recently, it has further hindered the construction of five battleships. In addition to actively building ships, the United States is also following in the footsteps of Great Britain, announcing the reservation of 59,000 tons of destroyers whose ship age has exceeded the limit. France is also unwilling to lag behind. Even when its finances are extremely tight, it still does not hesitate to raise huge debts to expand its armaments and implement a shipbuilding plan. Japan announced the abandonment of the naval treaties two years ago and actively accumulated materials, preparing to implement a large-scale shipbuilding plan starting next year, in order to bring its military strength to the same level as Great Britain and the United States. The naval budget for next year has reached 680 million yuan, setting a record. In the past two years, Italy has built two battleships of 35,000 tons and many light ships. There are currently more than 50 various ships under construction. As for Germany and the Soviet Union, they are stepping up the construction of the naval power that the Anglo-German and Anglo-Soviet agreements allow them to retain. Not only that, but the issue of the re-fortification of Great Britain, the United States, and Japan in the Pacific is unfolding, and the rivalry between Great Britain and Italy in the Mediterranean is also becoming more active. The latter issue may be temporarily eased by the conclusion of the Anglo-Italian Mediterranean Gentleman's Agreement, but the former issue is becoming more serious. Not long ago, Great Britain had a proposal to maintain Article 19 of the Washington Naval Treaty, restricting fortification of the Pacific. However, this proposal was not accepted by Japan and the United States. Recently, the United States has built air force bases on Midway Island and Wake Island in the Pacific as a countermeasure against Japan's arms expansion. In this way, it will be much easier for the United States to fight in the Western Pacific in the future. This has also given Japan a major stimulus for arms expansion.

In short, the naval powers' arms expansion competition is becoming more and more obvious. This competition can easily evolve into a maritime arms race. After the expiration of the two major naval treaties, what methods should be used to reduce the dangers of this naval competition? This should be the question that statesmen from all countries who care about world peace are anxious about.

End of the Japan-Australia Trade War, Exchange of Notes Stipulates Trade Relations, Valid for Eighteen Months 41

(Tokyo) End of the Japan-Australia Trade War, Exchange of Notes Stipulates Trade Relations, Valid for Eighteen Months

(Tokyo) The Japan-Australia trade negotiations have been completely resolved with the exchange of official documents between the representatives of the two countries on the 26th. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs specially announced the contents of the announcement on the evening of the 27th as follows. The Australian Minister to Japan, Mr. Garret's note to Consul General Murai,

(1) The Australian government abolishes the import permit system implemented on July 8, 1936, for Japanese goods.

(2) The Australian government applies the intermediate tax rate to Japanese-made cotton cloth and rayon cloth.

(3) The Australian government reduces the intermediate tax rate for cotton cloth and rayon cloth as follows: Cotton cloth per square yard

One and a quarter pence for bleached cotton cloth, one and a half pence

Two pence for printed cotton cloth, four pence for rayon cloth

(4) The Australian government waives the 5% ad valorem tax on Japanese-made cotton cloth and rayon cloth.

(5) From January 1, 1937, to June 31, 1938, the Australian government will allow 76,675,000 square yards of Japanese cotton cloth and rayon cloth. Consul General Murai's note to Minister Garret,

(1) The Japanese government abolishes the 5% additional ad valorem tax and import permit system stipulated in Imperial Ordinance No. 124 of Showa 11 (1936).

(2) The Japanese government will allow the import of 800,000 bales of Australian wool until June 30, 1938. During this period, wool that is approved for import but expires and arrives in Japan will be allowed to enter the country if it arrives in Japan before September 30, 1938. (3) During the period from January 1, 1937, to June 30, 1938, the Japanese government will limit the quantity of Japanese cotton cloth and rayon cloth shipped to Australia as follows: 76,875,000 square yards of cotton cloth and 76,875,000 square yards of rayon cloth. (28th Alliance)

Melbourne, the Australian-Japanese trade war, ended formally today because both parties have completed their new commerce terms. The agreed term of this item is eighteen months, to June 30, 1938 expiry. The Australia and Japan trade war, has been in place since May this year. At that time, the Australian nation had, for imports on Japanese goods such as cotton cloth and rayon, increased commercial tax rates, and implemented a licensing system, Its purpose was to increase commercial preference for England, and to support its own country’s products. Japan was greatly affected as a result, and immediately followed the procedure of dealing with Canada, to reciprocate. As a result, Australian wheat, wool, and flour must be licensed to be imported into Japan, and for a certain number of goods imported into Japan, a tax rate of 50% must be added. Japan also threatened to reduce the number of Australian wool imports by two-thirds, and purchase one-third from other countries, with the remainder using artificial fibers as a substitute. (Reuters, 27th)

German General Seekt Dies, Once Served as Military Advisor to Our Country 45

(Berlin) General Hans von Seekt, a famous German general who reorganized the German army after the European War and served as a military advisor to the Chinese government from 1934 to 1935, died today at the age of 67. The victories of the German army during the European War were largely due to Seekt's efforts. When the European War broke out, Seekt served as the chief of staff of General Lottau, commander of the Third Army. In 1914, he participated in the battles of the Western Front. In January 1915, he planned the German army's offensive in Soissons. Later, he served as the chief of staff of General Mackensen and planned the strategy to defeat the enemy forces in Galicia, allowing them to drive deep into Serbia. In 1920, when the Kapp Putsch occurred in Germany, Seekt used his iron fist to suppress it. Later, he completed the reorganization of the Republican National Defense Force. During this campaign, Seekt dealt with difficulties with a calm and decisive spirit. A slight mistake would have been enough to cause a greater revolution. Seekt has since gained international fame. Afterwards, Seekt announced that if anyone, regardless of their political party, attempted to take action again, he would order the troops to open fire. Seekt kept his word, so everyone was in awe of him. However, this angered many conservatives, and Seekt became the target of all the monarchists. In 1926, Seekt was slandered for allowing Prince Wilhelm, the eldest son of the former Crown Prince, to participate in the army maneuvers, and he resigned angrily in October of that year. Seekt was the son of a general and had a solid family education, so he showed his talent as soon as he joined the army and was promoted very quickly, holding important positions. On the day he resigned from his command of the army, he ordered his subordinates to bid farewell and ordered the German army to work diligently at all times, maintain the honor of the German military, until they entered the grave. Seekt's loyalty to the country was praised by both the extreme left and the extreme right, which shows his trust in the whole country. In 1923, when Hitler launched a coup in Munich, President Ebert granted Seekt full authority, and Seekt was able to restore order in a short period of time. Seekt was a resolute and taciturn person. Whether he was a monarchist, a liberal, or a democrat, even his closest friends did not know. However, judging from his words and deeds in peacetime, he seemed to be a monarchist, because Seekt not only respected the former emperor, but also believed that a unified Germany under the Prussian emperor had the best chance of restoring its world status. (Reuters, 28th)

(Berlin) General Hans von Seekt, a famous German general during the European War, died this afternoon at the age of 70. Seekt was born in 1866. He joined the army at the age of 19 and served in the military until 1913, when he served as the chief of staff of the Third Army. After the outbreak of the Great War, he served as the chief of staff of the famous General Mackensen, commanding operations in Serbia, Romania, and Galicia. Later, he was hired by Turkey as the chief of staff of the Turkish army. After the end of the war, he participated in the German delegation to the Treaty of Versailles. In 1920, he organized the German National Defense Force and was appointed as the commander-in-chief. In 1926, he retired after allowing the grandson of the deposed Emperor Wilhelm II to join the National Defense Force, which caused resentment from the republican government at the time. He joined the right-wing People's Party and engaged in political activities. From 1930 to 1932, he served as a member of the House of Representatives. Later, he was hired by the Chinese government as a military advisor for more than a year. During his lifetime, he advocated that the army's organization should be centered on long-term professional soldiers and supplemented by short-term conscripts. This view is still supported by some people in Germany. General Seekt wrote many books, and "The Thoughts of a Soldier" is widely praised at the time. (Havas, 27th)

Spanish Rebels Fiercely Attack the Capital, Meeting Setbacks; Nationalists Valiantly Counterattack, Both Sides Suffering Heavy Casualties 46

Madrid – National Army: Today, under the cover of artillery fire, a swarm of troops charged across the Manzanares River, launching a fierce attack on the thinly manned and unprepared defense forces. They succeeded in capturing the North Station. However, the government forces immediately dispatched reinforcements, transporting them by automobile to the Western Front for a counterattack. Eventually, they drove the National Army back to the areas of Carabanchel and Barajas de Jarama. The government forces claimed that this counterattack advanced one mile. The International Brigades have now occupied El Pardo. The government forces on the northern route also hold a slight advantage. The National Army abandoned several tanks while retreating, but the National Army leader denies this claim. (National Dispatch, 27th)

Madrid – Fierce battles erupted today in the suburbs of Madrid, the fiercest since the siege of Madrid began. The National Army crossed the Manzanares River near the Parque de la Casa de Campo in the western suburbs, pressing towards the capital. Meanwhile, the government forces advanced two kilometers near the town of Usera in the southern suburbs, threatening the right flank of the National Army. The details are as follows: On the western front, the National Army launched an offensive near the Parque de la Casa de Campo this morning, immediately crossing the Manzanares River, opening artillery fire, and attacking the positions of the government forces, supported by six tanks. The government forces returned fire with artillery. Subsequently, the militia charged out of their trenches for a counterattack, engaging in hand-to-hand combat with the Moroccan indigenous troops and foreign legion soldiers of the National Army until 6:30 PM, eventually driving back the National Army. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. Two National Army tanks fell into the river. At the same time, on the southern front, the government forces launched an offensive in the town of Usera. At 7:30 AM, the sound of artillery rumbled as the government forces began their charge. The militia forces surged out of their trenches, divided into two columns, advancing valiantly under the cover of machine guns. By 4:00 PM, they had advanced two kilometers and occupied the town of Basurillas. After consolidating their newly occupied positions, they continued fighting. After the government forces occupied Basurillas, their artillery units could bombard the National Army positions in the Parque de la Casa de Campo in the western suburbs, and threaten the town of Carabanchel. (Havas Dispatch, 27th)

Madrid – The Nationalist forces shelled the densely populated Latina district of the capital from 3:00 AM until 10:30 AM this morning, the shelling was initially sparse but intensified suddenly at 7:00 AM. The residents of the area immediately sought refuge in cellars. Some women, disregarding the danger, still crowded into shops to buy food, but were eventually dispersed by the militia. According to news received here from the northern port of Bilbao, the Nationalist forces launched a fierce attack on Markina in the Basque region, but were repulsed by the government forces. Britain to Build World's Largest Battleship, Costing £8 Million 50

(London) The Daily Express reports that the British Admiralty will soon build the world's largest battleship, costing £8 million, more than £1 million more than the battleships "King George V" and "Prince of Wales" built after the expiration of the London Naval Treaty. The huge cost is due to the ship's need for fully equipped anti-aircraft guns. This world's largest battleship may soon have two sister ships built. (National Dispatch, 28th)

(Nanjing) The Washington and London treaties will be completely abolished in three days, and the world will enter the first year of treaty-free naval freedom. Within the year, an understanding has been reached between the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan regarding the application of the trapezoidal clause to auxiliary vessels that should be abandoned. The results are as follows:

The United Kingdom retains four Hawkins-class Class A cruisers and modifies five Ceres-class cruisers, and also retains 40,000 tons of destroyers exceeding their age.

The United States, like the United Kingdom, retains 40,000 tons of destroyers and adds 19,000 tons, totaling nearly 60,000 tons of destroyers.

Japan, of course, can retain 28,000 tons for the United Kingdom's 40,000 tons of destroyers.

Since Japan's destroyers have already been abandoned, and there are currently only 11,000 tons of destroyers, it is agreed to retain 15,000 tons of submarines. As for submarines, in accordance with the wishes of the United States, it has expressed a magnanimous attitude and applied the trapezoidal clause. In this way, the ships that the navies of the United Kingdom and the United States want to retain and can use can be retained without being abandoned. Even with submarines, they can stand in an advantageous position. As a result, the ships abandoned at the end of 1936 are generally not abandoned. Also, in the first year of treaty-free navy, the current strength of the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan is as follows (excluding those under construction, unit tons):

Battleships

Japan 272,070 9 ships

United States 455,400 15 ships

United Kingdom 474,750 same as above

Aircraft Carriers

Japan 68,370 4 ships

United States 92,000 4 ships

United Kingdom 115,350 6 ships

Auxiliary Vessels

Japan 405,677 189 ships

United States 515,345 330 ships

United Kingdom 627,934 276 ships

Total

Japan 746,27 202 ships

Japan-Russia Fishing Treaty Extended for One Year, Protocol Signed 51

(Tokyo) The protocol regarding the extension of the validity of the Japan-Soviet Fisheries Treaty was passed by the Privy Council Congress on the morning of the 28th. The government immediately submitted it to the cabinet for decision and requested the Emperor's approval. The Foreign Minister then telegraphed Ambassador Shigemitsu in the afternoon to sign it. As a result, the protocol was decided to be formally signed in Moscow by Ambassador Shigemitsu and Foreign Affairs Director Stomoniakov, in accordance with the contact between Japan and the Soviet Union. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs will publish the full text of the protocol as soon as it receives a telegram confirming the completion of the signing. Due to the conclusion of the protocol between Japan and the Soviet Union on the 28th, the basic fisheries relationship between Japan and the Soviet Union can be said to have been satisfactorily adjusted. The Soviet Union voluntarily maintained the stability and extension of the fishing area under the Hirota-Ganin Agreement and the issue of the ruble conversion rate of three jiao and two fen and five li, which had been agreed upon between Japan and the Soviet Union. The Soviet People's Commissariat for the Food Industry instructed the Vladivostok Far East Fisheries Administration. The specific content of this resolution is as follows:

Conversion rate issue: The conversion rate of one ruble to three jiao and two fen and five li will continue to be paid as before for borrowing area fees and other expenses.

Fishing area issues

(1) Among the stable fishing areas under the Hirota-Ganin Agreement, those expiring within this year will continue to be extended for one year. Japan will continue to retain 282 fishing areas as before.

(2) The auctioned fishing areas, only those expiring within this year, will be auctioned on February 28 next year.

(3) New fishing areas will be auctioned on February 28 next year.

(4) The contract period for factory fishing areas (special contract fishing areas) is July of the year after next and will of course be retained by Japan.

(5) Soviet state-owned fishing areas, recognized by the Hirota-Ganin Agreement, will continue to be valid. (Allied News Agency Dispatch, 28th)

Japan Continues Four-Minister Conference to Reform Central Institutions 52

(Tokyo) The fifth four-ministry meeting to review and adjust the reform of central institutions was held at the residence of the Minister of Finance on the afternoon of the 28th. The four relevant cabinet members, including Minister of Finance Baba, Minister of Education Hirao, Minister of Communications Raimogi, and Minister of Railways Maeda, attended. Following previous discussions on the draft for the establishment of a new state policy integration agency, the Cabinet General Affairs Agency, a general outline has gradually emerged. The general opinions are as follows: The name of the new agency is the Cabinet General Affairs Agency. The Director-General of General Affairs should be treated the same as a minister appointed by the Emperor. The General Affairs Agency will have three bureaus: the Planning Bureau (reorganizing the current Cabinet Investigation Bureau, Resources Bureau, and Statistics Bureau), the Personnel Bureau, and the Budget Bureau. The Personnel Bureau and the Budget Bureau will not be subordinate to the General Affairs Agency. The Personnel Bureau will be an independent bureau, located in the Cabinet. Also, the Budget Bureau will not be established and will continue to be handled by the current Budget Bureau of the Ministry of Finance. However, the General Affairs Agency will be involved in the budget for implementing state policy. The Legal System Bureau and the Information Committee will remain as before. As for the relationship between the Economic Conference of the Economic Staff Headquarters and the General Affairs Agency, they will remain linked and will not be regarded as the relationship between the Cabinet Review Committee and the Investigation Bureau. (Allied Dispatch, 28th)

Fire in German Subway, Construction Began Three Years Ago, Still Not Completed, Goering and Goebbels Visit the Scene 53

(Berlin) The underground railway at Potsdamer Platz was started after the Nazi Party came to power and has been under construction for more than three years. Today, a fire suddenly broke out in the railway workshop and spread rapidly. Thick smoke continuously billowed from the ground. Although 19 fire hoses worked together to put out the fire, the fire had not subsided slightly by 10:00 PM. The material losses were huge. The fire brigade excavated trenches in the nearby Leipzig Street so that the power of the fire hoses could directly reach the fire pit. Minister of Aviation General Goering and Minister of Propaganda Dr. Goebbels also arrived at the scene. Philippines Economic Progress, Rich Gold Production 55

(Washington) The International Trade Magazine published an article today praising the economic situation of the Philippines as having made great progress. The article is based on a report by Leech, the US Commercial Representative stationed in Manila, stating that all industries in the Philippines have made progress in the first nine months of this year, indicating that the prosperity of the Philippines has gradually recovered. The financial situation of the autonomous government is very good, and all tax revenues have increased compared with last year. Customs duties have increased by more than one-third, and gold production is also improving day by day. 1.5 million tons of raw gold ore have been refined in nine months, and the annual output should reach 44 million pesos. People's interest in other minerals, such as copper, iron, and chromium, has also increased. This year's foreign trade has reached the highest peak in five years. Exports in the past nine months totaled 216,774,000 pesos, an increase of 51% compared with last year. Imports were 150,143,000 pesos, also an increase of 21%. The trade surplus has tripled compared to last year. (National Dispatch, 27th)

Because the employer has already implemented a 40-hour work week, they will not allow extra holidays during Christmas and New Year. (Reuters Dispatch, 28th)

French Labor-Management Compulsory Arbitration Law Passed by Senate with Amendments 57

(Paris) The government's proposed bill on compulsory arbitration of labor-management disputes has been discussed back and forth in the Senate and the House of Representatives for several resolutions, but it has not yet been definitively passed. According to the bill, it was passed by the House of Representatives in accordance with the original government proposal on the first of this month, and then after being amended by the Senate on the 18th, it was sent back to the House of Representatives for reconsideration. The House of Representatives passed a new clause on the 23rd and submitted it to the Senate for review. The Senate then handed it over to the Committee on Commerce and Labor yesterday for re-examination and drafted new clauses. Today, the Senate slightly amended the clauses and passed them with a majority of 170 votes to 89 votes. Therefore, the bill must be returned to the House of Representatives for review before a final decision can be made. The clauses passed by the Senate still differ from the clauses of the House of Representatives, which stipulate that full power is granted to the government until June 1, 1937, so as to determine the method of arbitration and mediation. This method is published by order of the Council of State. If the opinions of the two parties in the dispute, or between the arbitrators, cannot be consistent, the Supreme Court or the various courts of appeal will separately appoint arbitrators from industrial and commercial groups to rule on it. These arbitrators should respect the rights of both labor and management to determine an appropriate solution to the dispute. The so-called rights of both labor and management include property rights, the right to organize trade unions, the right to individual freedom of work, and the right to freedom of trade unions. Once the arbitrator makes a ruling, both labor and management should abide by it, and it must be enforced and made public. When the Senate began discussing the bill today, Prime Minister Léon Blum personally attended and delivered a speech, objecting to the provision in the draft of the Committee on Commerce and Labor that "employers have the right to individual dismissal in addition to what the arbitrator has decided," saying that this provision is detrimental to the rights of workers and is biased towards one party. The result will not only fail to ease labor unrest, but will increase disputes. In short, a part of the employers are determined to oppose the arbitration system and want to cancel the concessions made by the capital side to the labor side in June of this year. I hope that the senators will not allow this trend to grow. "Because our ambition is to maintain the harmony between labor and management. What is the way to maintain it? Is it by coercion? Then I say, what we want is a method of social peace. Only this method is suitable for the feelings of the French people and the needs of the international community. It should be known that the maintenance of international peace depends first on the maintenance of internal order in France and the coordination of labor and management." Léon Blum went on to praise the General Confederation of Labor, saying that its efforts to stop labor-management disputes are indeed commendable. Finally, the Senate accepted the Prime Minister's opinion and deleted the section in the draft that employers have the right to individual dismissal, and then voted to pass it. (Havas Dispatch, 27th)

Foreign Rice Tax Not Approved for Repeal: Guangdong Province Actively Relieving the Rice Shortage, Raising 5 Million to Purchase Rice from Anhui and Hunan, Implementing Rural Loans to Increase Production 64

Guangzhou Dispatch: The poor late-rice harvest in Guangdong Province this year has led to soaring rice prices and widespread suffering among the poor. Considering that the winter defense period is approaching, with many unemployed, coupled with the high cost of living, those without stable employment or property are bound to resort to desperate measures for the sake of survival, which will greatly impact social order. Therefore, the military and civilian authorities previously telegraphed the central government, requesting a temporary repeal of the foreign rice tax to facilitate the import of foreign rice and alleviate the food shortage. However, the central government replied that it could not be approved. Consequently, the authorities are seeking alternative remedies, formulating comprehensive measures to address the rice shortage in both the short and long term, proceeding on multiple fronts. The short-term measures involve the Department of Finance convening representatives from the Department of Civil Affairs, the Department of Construction, the Central Bank branch, the Communications Bank branch, the Bank of China branch, and the provincial bank to resolve the establishment of a People's Food Regulation Committee, raising 5 million yuan. The Department of Finance will advance 1 million yuan, with the remaining 4 million yuan to be contributed as loans by various banks in Guangdong Province at reasonable interest rates. This 5 million yuan will be used to purchase rice from Anhui and Hunan provinces to be transported to Guangdong, regulating the food supply in place of foreign rice imports. The committee is scheduled to be established on the 28th, with 15 members, including the governor of Guangdong Province, Huang Musong, the pacification director, Yu Hanmou, the director of the Department of Finance, Song Ziliang, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Wang Yingyu, the director of the Department of Construction, Liu Weizhi, the mayor of Guangzhou, Zeng Yangfu, the representative of the Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce, Zou Dianbang, the Rice and Sugar Guild, Han Zhuofu, and representatives from the banking sector, Zhong E, Chen Yuqian, Wen Wanqing, Gu Yiqun, Shen Jing, Wu Kejia, Zhu Ruquan, etc. Huang Musong, Song Ziliang, Chen Yuqian, Gu Yiqun, and Zhong E will serve as standing committee members. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to Shanghai, requesting the Central Bank to entrust the Central Trust Bureau to purchase 20,000 piculs of Wuhu rice from Anhui. As for the 200,000 bags of white rice purchased by Guangdong rice merchants in Hunan some days ago, which were being obstructed by the Hunan Provincial Inspection Bureau, Committee Member Song Ziliang telegraphed He in Hunan yesterday, requesting assistance to facilitate the early transport south for regulation. Once the People's Food Regulation Committee is established and the bank loans are secured, large quantities of rice will be ordered from Anhui and Hunan successively. Regarding Hunan Province, the committee will also pursue a salt-for-rice exchange between Guangdong and Hunan to facilitate trade and address shortages. Currently, both sides are drafting a contract. To fundamentally alleviate the food crisis, the authorities have decided to start by assisting rural areas, providing farmers with loans to increase rural capital and boost rice production, with the goal of achieving food self-sufficiency. Regarding rural loans, the provincial government will first establish a Rural Cooperative Affairs Committee, responsible for management. The committee will send personnel to various villages to guide farmers in forming cooperatives, which will be responsible for receiving and disbursing loans and managing agricultural product mortgages. As for the loan method, the provincial government has decided to allocate a portion of the revenue from tobacco and alcohol excise taxes and stamp duties as capital, dividing the province into ten loan districts. Nine counties, including Shixing in the Northern River region, have been designated as the first batch of loan districts, with a loan amount of 990,000 yuan, allocated as follows: Group 1: Shixing County 30,000 yuan, Nanxiong 200,000 yuan; Group 2: Heshan 350,000 yuan, Xinhui 100,000 yuan; Group 3: Qingyuan 220,000 yuan, Sihui 10,000 yuan; Group 4: Conghua 50,000 yuan, Huaxian 8,000 yuan; Group 5: Yunfu 12,000 yuan. After receiving the order, the Rural Cooperative Affairs Committee dispatched staff member Wang Zhaoming yesterday to Shixing and other counties to guide the formation of cooperatives to facilitate loan disbursement. Telegrams were also sent to the magistrates of the above-mentioned counties for assistance (December 27).

Fuzhou Merchant Guilds' Measures to Alleviate Year-End Financial Difficulties: Financial Maintenance Association Formed by Merchants, Issuing 3 Million Yuan in Circulation Notes, Various Measures Drafted by Provincial Government 65

Fuzhou Dispatch: As the Lunar New Year is approaching, the financial situation in the Fuzhou business community is extremely difficult. Merchant guilds have convened a meeting of representatives and decided to request the provincial government to forward a request to the Central Bank, Bank of China, Communications Bank, and Farmers Bank to jointly allocate 5 million yuan for merchants to borrow against real estate collateral. If the four banks cannot implement this, they request permission for the merchants to organize a financial maintenance association, with the merchants providing real estate as collateral, issuing 3 million yuan in circulation notes. The provincial government has forwarded this to the Legislative Affairs Office for review, which has drafted ten measures: (1) A bill and credit maintenance association should be jointly organized by money shops and commercial firms with economic capacity (or a bill acceptance office, bill discounting office, or other name); (2) The bill and credit maintenance association shall be managed by the business community, but the government may send personnel to assist; (3) Commercial firms meeting the requirements of item 1 may join the bill maintenance association at any time. Participants may freely determine a capital contribution amount and provide property equivalent to the participation amount as security. The aforementioned property must be registered and cannot be freely transferred or used as other security during the organizational period; (4) Commercial firms participating in the bill maintenance association may issue or accept bills within the total amount of their registered property; (5) Commercial firms participating in the maintenance association may issue bills when extending loans or repaying debts; (6) Commercial firms participating in the maintenance association must submit bills for issuance or acceptance to the maintenance association for review and approval; (7) Bills approved for issuance according to the preceding item may specify several other participating commercial firms to endorse; (8) Commercial firms participating in the maintenance association shall deposit a portion of the interest earned from issuing, accepting, or endorsing bills with the maintenance association as a fund to compensate for bill losses. If there is a surplus, it shall be distributed proportionally according to the capital contribution amount when the association is dissolved; (9) The maintenance association shall compensate member commercial firms for losses incurred due to bill debts, supplementing any shortfall after legally assisting them in seeking compensation, from the accumulated fund in the preceding item; (10) Disputes arising from bills shall be handled swiftly by an arbitration body organized by the government and the chamber of commerce. The provincial government replied that if the above measures can be effectively implemented, the issuance and payment of bills will have adequate security. The business community will surely be happy to use them, and discounting at banks will also be easy. The government can provide strong assistance within its capabilities. Once the foundation is solid, circulation will naturally expand, and it can replace a portion of the banknotes. Its security is even better than circulation notes. It can maintain itself even without borrowing from banks. The government immediately forwarded these measures to the chamber of commerce for review and implementation. The chamber of commerce convened executive and supervisory committee members and representatives from various merchant guilds on the 25th, starting the meeting at 9 AM and concluding at 4 PM. The merchants deeply appreciated the government's efforts to safeguard commerce and generally agreed with the ten principles. However, they believed that the total amount and duration of bank discounting must be clearly defined before implementation can begin. It was decided to request the government to negotiate two points with the banks: (1) Discounting should be available at any time, up to a total amount of 3 million yuan; (2) The duration should be limited to one year. Chamber of Commerce Chairman Luo Mianhou, Standing Committee Member Hong Fasui, and Supervisory Committee Member Lin Chuncheng were appointed to consult with the Legislative Affairs Office of the provincial government again at 10 AM on the 26th to facilitate the early establishment of the bill and credit maintenance association and smoothly overcome the year-end financial difficulties (December 26).

Major Renovation of the Seawall 70

This county is located near the river and sea, and the dikes are often in danger. Although they have been renovated over the years, the time constraints and lack of funds have prevented them from being perfect. In order to ensure the safety of the lives and property of hundreds of thousands of residents in Jiangnan, it has been decided to carry out a major renovation. The materials will all be Songjiang Bixie Mountain stone and Jianmu wood. The section of the Daotang Temple is the largest project, requiring 1,822 cubic meters of stone and 1,082 wooden stakes. The total cost is estimated at 90,000 yuan. The construction plan has been submitted to the province for approval. The transportation of materials has been contracted to the public and private sectors. It is expected to be completed next summer.

Suzhou: Expanding Publicity and Investigating Opium Offenders 71

The Wu County government is expanding publicity and actively carrying out a general re-examination of opium offenders. It has ordered the district offices to instruct the township, town, and Baojia to promote awareness by carrying signs and gongs. Opium offenders can surrender and quit before January 4 to avoid punishment. A coffin parade will be held on the Lunar New Year. The general re-examination period is set from January 6 to January 31. During this period, all township, town, and Baojia leaders will be mobilized to investigate house by house. If opium offenders are found, they will be arrested and severely punished.

Wuxi: Reforming Land Tax Collection 72

The Jiangsu Department of Finance recently convened a meeting of accounting directors from all counties in the province. Wuxi County Accounting Director Jiang also went to the province to participate. He returned to Wuxi yesterday. According to him, many cases were discussed at the meeting, and there were three special cases related to Wuxi: (1) In the future, deed tax revenue should be collected by the tax collection office of the Farmers Bank, and separate five-part receipts should be used; (2) Starting from the collection of the second term land tax this year, all notices should be forwarded to the grain households by the township and town offices and should no longer be handled by the Tuzheng; (3) Financial tax police must find a guarantor. When going to the countryside to urge collection, they must wear a symbol for identification to avoid unscrupulous elements extorting money in the name of the tax police. The above points must be publicized and strictly followed.

Retired Soldier Brutally Murdered 73

Li Desheng, a Hunan native who previously served in the army, recently retired and rented a thatched shed from Wang Pan in Huihe Town, Wuxi. He lived alone and made a living by selling vegetables. He was suddenly murdered on a Gaotian near Huisheng Bridge. The Tuzheng Niu Wenyao, in cooperation with the Baojia leader, reported to the local court, which sent a prosecutor to investigate. It was found that the deceased had been pressed face down on the ground and strangled to death with a rope. The rope marks on his neck were obvious. They then went to the deceased's residence for a thorough inspection and ordered that a coffin be prepared for burial, pending the arrest and investigation of the murderer.

Changshu: Holding an Art Performance to Aid Suiyuan 74

Bengbu: Preparing to Establish a Meteorological Observatory 76

Meteorological undertakings are closely related to important government policies such as farmland water conservancy and aviation. The Huai River Basin in northern Anhui urgently needs meteorological equipment. The Meteorological Observatory of the Academia Sinica planned to establish a third-class observatory in Bengbu long ago, but it has not been realized due to limited financial resources. It is learned that the provincial government originally planned to establish the Anhui Meteorological Observatory, and has decided to allocate 150 yuan per month to the Bengbu third-class meteorological observatory for recurring expenses starting from January 26. The preparation for establishment and the required equipment will still be separately planned and allocated by the Central Meteorological Institute.

Reorganization of the Water and Land Public Security Bureau 77

The Bengbu Public Security Bureau was originally named the Bengbu Police Department, and the Changhuai Water Public Security Bureau was originally named the Changhuai Water Police Department. The current names were changed in the 16th year of the Republic of China, when the National Revolutionary Army recovered northern Anhui. The two water and land bureaus recently received orders from the province to change to police bureaus from January 1 of the following year. The two bureaus have sent personnel to the province to receive new seals for implementation. The Changjing symbols will also be replaced uniformly.

Famous Drug Trafficker Apprehended 78

Famous drug trafficker Wu Tinggui, along with Qin Zixiu, who was captured in Bengbu, are important figures in the local drug trade, within the so-called "Four King Kongs." He was previously arrested and held in Fengyang Prison. Wu was released from prison not long ago and resumed his old business, trafficking in large quantities of drugs and secretly selling them in northern Anhui. The Public Security Bureau learned of this and had detectives arrest Wu at the Hebei Bus Station on the 25th. Four packages of coffee essence were found in his suitcase, and 21 packages of heroin were found in his net basket. The witnesses were taken to the bureau for investigation.

Random Notes from Europe (3) 79

— Our European Correspondent, Lieshan

9. Sacrificing for the Country—General Göring Loses Twenty Pounds

For the past two or three years, Germany has been experiencing "food panics" several times every winter, such as shortages of butter, eggs, meat, etc. Some say that this is a pre-planned scheme by the German military authorities, serving as a kind of national defense test. Others say that the reason lies in Germany's lack of foreign exchange, which reduces the import of butter and other items. The Nazi Party's famous internal propaganda slogan is, "Guns instead of butter." National defense is more important than everything, hoping the people will be patient. The winter of 1936 arrived. General Göring was appointed by Hitler at this time, with full authority to handle Germany's four-year economic plan. The main point of General Göring's first speech was to advise people to "tighten their belts" and cooperate with him to overcome this difficulty together. Germany lacks raw materials, and other countries cannot understand Germany's plight in this regard, so Germany is forced to invent a raw material substitute by using its own chemical industry. He also guaranteed that in four years, Germany's artificial industrial raw materials would definitely be self-sufficient.

Regarding the food problem—lack of eggs, General Göring said that nature is naturally like this. Hens sometimes lay eggs and sometimes they don't. Conversely, people don't have a reason to eat eggs every day. The next day, a Nazi Party newspaper added a large headline to this section: "The government cannot lay eggs."

Secondly, regarding butter, General Göring said that he has recently lost twenty pounds of weight because he often has to do without butter. However, this sentence was not published in German newspapers the next day.

It is speculated that General Göring's weight is about two hundred and fifty pounds—

10. More on General Göring

Among the many important figures in the German National Socialist Party, one of the most popular is General Göring. General Göring holds countless important positions. His titles include Premier of Prussia, Minister of Aviation, Air Force General, Speaker of the German Parliament, Chief of the Political Police, First German Forest Supervisor, First German Hunting Governor, Person in Charge of the Four-Year Economic Plan... and so on. In addition, he is the Director of Prussian Theaters. His new wife, whom he married last year, is an actress.

General Göring loves military uniforms, and his position just happens to provide him with countless uniforms to change into. Therefore, in Berlin social circles or German illustrated magazines, you can often see General Göring and his various military uniforms. General Göring loves medals, and a large number of medals are inseparable from him, just like his military uniforms. There is a large medal that he received during the European War. During the European War, General Göring was a very famous air force officer.

General Göring's position in the Third Reich is second only to Hitler. Many people believe that he is Hitler's future successor. Although he is one of the main figures in the Nazi Party, he usually only pays special attention to military affairs. It can be said that Germany currently possesses a powerful air force thanks to his personal contributions. However, he is not particularly interested in the newly emerging theories of the Nazi Party. In the Nazi Party, he is one of the figures with the least anti-Semitic sentiment.

General Göring's personality can sometimes make people afraid, but sometimes he seems amiable. Over the years, there have been thousands of political jokes circulating among the German people, and most of them are about General Göring. According to a certain reporter who often interacts with General Göring, General Göring once told him that he had ordered his adjutant to collect such jokes and report them to him every day. The subject matter of the jokes mostly involves General Göring's military uniforms and medals. An example:

"Hitler went to the theater one day with General Göring. The scheduled time had passed when Hitler arrived, but General Göring was nowhere to be seen. The male lead on stage, seeing the leader arrive, hurriedly went backstage to greet him without changing his clothes. When he entered the box, Hitler mistook him for General Göring. Hitler said, 'Another new uniform, Hermann (General Göring's nickname). Don't make a fool of yourself!'"

The name Hermann is very common among the German people. Germans often say, "Our Hermann," instead of calling him "General Göring." It is said that General Göring is the most tolerant person in the Nazi Party when it comes to political jokes. When he got married last year, the president of the German Journalists Association informed all members that each person had to write a joke about General Göring and send it directly to him as a congratulatory message, although later no German reporter dared to try.

11. The Art of Propaganda

"It is said that Dr. Goebbels, the German Minister of Propaganda, once sent someone to Mussolini to ask about the art of propaganda: what methods should be used to make people believe? Mussolini said: 'That is a very easy thing to do, that is, the first thing you say to the people must be the truth. After that, no matter how many lies you tell, people will believe you. For example, if the Italian expeditionary force in Abyssinia actually lost three hundred people in a battle, then we will tell the people that our army lost two hundred and fifty people on a certain day, or simply report the facts, because it is the truth, people will definitely believe this sentence. Then we can propagandize whatever we want.' But Dr. Goebbels still found it troublesome and was reluctant to even tell the first truth!"

Smart readers will naturally see that this is also a type of German political joke.

Speaking of the success of the Nazi Party today, we must admire Dr. Goebbels' propaganda genius. Moreover, his position in the Third Reich is only second to General Göring. However, although Dr. Goebbels controls Germany's overall propaganda apparatus, judging by his personal achievements, he does not seem to be as good as the military-style General Göring. At least he has not achieved the point where people would call him "Our Joseph" (the Doctor’s nickname). It is said that he once tried to popularize the term "Our Doctor" among the German people, but it also failed. The reason is that everyone is a little wary and doesn't dare to speak ill of him. His greatest enemy in life is foreign correspondents stationed in Germany, because these reporters often expose his propaganda tricks.

Conversely, General Göring is a true propagandist. He knows that the German people love military uniforms and medals, so he turns himself into the center of political jokes and lets people spread them. The more jokes there are, the more popular General Göring becomes among the people. Only jokes about him can be heard semi-publicly in German cafes and taverns. When he got married, a Berlin news vendor shouted on the street, "Our Hermann is finally married. Why should he be more comfortable than us?" A news vendor can use this kind of language for advertising, which shows how popular General Göring is.

A German said, "We advocate a protectionist tariff policy for the 'export' of General Göring. If other countries want to use him. As for Dr. Goebbels, we not only promote 'free trade,' but even 'encourage exports.'" Here, it seems that we can see the different propaganda methods of each person.

A hotshot who once served as the director of the intelligence department of a certain country's Ministry of Foreign Affairs once told a reporter how difficult it is to announce political news. He said: "When we spread a piece of news, it must not be seen as a lie for at least three weeks. If it is discovered after three weeks, then in fact our propaganda is considered successful. Because people generally don't pay much attention to things from three weeks ago, but only this period of three weeks, in the eyes of people in our bureau, is already longer than three months!"

Propaganda is truly an art!

12. The Nazi Party's Anti-Semitism

Opposition to Jews is clearly stated in the Nazi Party platform. The new laws promulgated at the Nazi Party Congress in Nuremberg last year not only stipulated that Jews are not allowed to marry people of Germanic descent, but even German female servants employed in Jewish homes who are under the age of forty-five are to be prohibited; even if the housewife in a family is of German descent and the husband is of Jewish descent, there are no exceptions. The reason lies in protecting the superior Germanic bloodline, so one must "prevent problems before they arise."

Our country's overseas Chinese wrestling master Huang Bochang, since returning to China, has fought three matches in Shanghai and won two, gaining a great reputation for a time, which has aroused the Chinese people's considerable understanding of the wrestling sport that they had previously ignored, and generated a strong interest. On Tuesday evening last week, when Mr. Huang defeated Indian master Piha Fan at St. George's on Du Mei Road, Afghan wrestling master Api Du jumped onto the stage and made wild remarks, setting a date for a challenge. At the same time, taking advantage of Huang's unpreparedness, he pushed him forcefully. Huang endured it and did not compete with him. At that time, the entire audience hated him and all booed him away. Api Du retreated in shame, but his heart was still unwilling. Mr. Huang also felt compelled to respond to the pressure and did not want to show weakness, so he especially scheduled a decisive battle to be held at the original location tonight at 8:30 PM, to compete with each other. The fight will consist of six rounds, each round lasting ten minutes. In addition, there will be a rematch between Mr. Huang's defeated opponent Piha Fan and Khabe Singh, who defeated Peterson, who defeated Akenado. Both people have great ambitions and hope to compete with Mr. Huang, so the battle between the two tonight is tantamount to paving the way for the upcoming bloody battle. The match will consist of four rounds, each round lasting two minutes. Ever since this news spread, people from all walks of life have been rushing to reserve seats. West Qing Basketball: Nanching Defeats St. John's; Qingguang Loses to Xintong 82

Three West Qing basketball games were held last night. Two were in the university division: Nanyang forfeited to Chizhi, and Nanching defeated St. John's by a large margin, 39-15. One was in the independent division: Xintong defeated Qingguang, 55-35. The first half was extremely intense, with Xintong only leading by five points, 23-18.

The Nanching-St. John's match turned into a one-sided affair. St. John's played disorganized and chaotic. Nanching took a 15-2 lead and finished the first half 20-8. In the second half, St. John's briefly showed signs of revival, but then retreated, ultimately losing 39-15 to Nanching's big win.

The Qingguang-Xintong game started next. Qingguang consisted of veterans of the arena. Although their physical strength may have declined, their form was still present. They were unhurried, completely different from the previous game, which was even more shocking. Qingguang took the lead all the way, 12-8, 14-10, 18-13. At this point, Xintong scored six consecutive points to take the lead. Lan Genlai Yin then scored four points, making the first half 23-19. In the second half, Qingguang's defense gradually loosened in terms of physical strength, and Xintong soared, scoring seventeen consecutive points after being up 27-24. Qingguang occasionally scored from then on, but it was of no use. The result was 55-35.

Thirteen-Mile Road Race: Important Information 83

Number Tags Will Also Be Issued

The city's Marathon Promotion Association is sponsoring the first 13-mile long-distance race, which is scheduled to be held in West Shanghai. A total of 156 people have signed up to participate. Race numbers have also been compiled, and number tags have been issued starting yesterday, so that racers can continue to pick up their number cloths at the original registration location. Recently, many parties from the city's political, government, and military circles have donated prizes, including a silver cup from Mayor Wu, a silver tripod from Director Pan, and fifteen silver cups and six silver shields from Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Min Bao, etc., which will be distributed to the winners. The association also announced six competition guidelines yesterday, which are transcribed as follows: (1) After receiving the number tag, racers can pick up their number cloth at the original registration location, but number tags cannot be reported as lost after they are lost. (2) Athletes should arrive on time for the start of the race to show the spirit of sportsmanship. (3) Number cloths should be pinned to the chest with four safety pins. (4) The assembly time is 7:30 AM on New Year's Day at the entrance of the Gan Gong School on Bailinan Road. If it rains, it will be postponed. (5) During the competition, shortcuts and irregular actions are not allowed midway, so as to respect personal integrity and sportsmanship. (6) If you are not familiar with the route, please pay attention to the clear signs placed by the association at the intersections during the competition.

More than a dozen people, including Leng Xueqiao, were elected as directors of the fifth session of the Shanghai Boy Scout Council. Afterwards, the Boy Scout representative gave a speech, stating that the Boy Scout cause should advance in both quality and quantity. The progress of Shanghai's Boy Scouts in terms of quantity has been quite rapid, but in terms of quality, it does not seem to be fully satisfactory. Everyone should pay attention to this. Representative Du gave a speech, saying that the spirit of the Boy Scouts is wisdom, benevolence, and courage. In the future, it is hoped that everyone will continue to focus on this spirit and strive for "good learning," "diligent practice," and "knowing shame." Tenth Anniversary of Jiaotong University Research Institute a Grand Occasion 96

The Research Institute of Jiaotong University in Shanghai was founded in 1926. This year marks its tenth anniversary. After several changes of date, the ceremony was finally held on the 28th of this month. Due to the ongoing national crisis, there was no extravagance. Only a luncheon was held at noon, and the various laboratories were opened to the public for viewing at 2:00 PM. A tea party was held at 4:00 PM to entertain the guests. On that day, there were dozens of attendees, including Ye Gongchuo, former Minister of Communications and Minister of Railways, Chen Jintao, former Minister of Finance and current Chairman of the Central Currency System Committee, Zhou Ren, representative of President Cai of the Academia Sinica, Liu Hongen of Shanghai University, Tang Wenkai of the Banking Association, Sheng Jun and Li Gan of the National Tariff Commission, and foreign guests Bu Fangji and Kang Deli. The ceremony was held at 11:00 AM in the Wen Zhi Hall of the university. First, Dr. Li Zhaohuan, the President of the university and Director of the institute, gave a report. Then, Mr. Ye delivered a speech, saying that the establishment of the Research Institute was one of the plans during his tenure as President of Jiaotong University. Today, it has achieved such results, which is beyond his expectations. He hopes that it will make further progress and establish contact with all aspects of the country to meet the needs of all aspects. Mr. Chen said that China's research spirit and inventive power have achieved amazing results in the past, but in the past two hundred years, it seems to have stagnated. In order to restore the past and promote the future, research institutes are greatly needed in China. Mr. Zhou briefly described the current situation of industrial research institutes in various countries and said that they are currently working hard, hoping that the Jiaotong University Research Institute will catch up quickly. The ceremony concluded at noon, and the meeting was adjourned after a photo was taken.

Social Affairs Bureau Regularly Holds Guidance for Further Education and Employment; January 10th Morning 97

The Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau issued an order to all public and private primary and secondary schools in the city yesterday, stating that in view of the case files taken over, the former Bureau of Education, for the purpose of guiding the graduating students of various primary and secondary schools in further education or employment, held lectures on guidance for further education and employment at the end of each semester. This business is actually to meet the actual needs of the schools, and should continue to be done. It has now ordered the schools to report the number of graduating students on file. According to the reports submitted by the schools to the Bureau, and after the distribution of venues, it is scheduled to be held at He'an and Shangwen Schools from 9:00 AM on January 10, 1937. However, since the schools are scattered throughout the city, it is difficult to concentrate all of them. It should be changed accordingly. All schools that have not been concentrated by the Bureau may hire lecturers and hold separate sessions, and report the handling situation to the Bureau for verification at any time. In addition to the schools that should be concentrated and participate, another order shall be issued, and a letter shall be sent to the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute to facilitate the hiring of lecturers for schools that cannot be concentrated and participate. This order shall be followed in its entirety.

When the time expired, the score was tied at thirteen to thirteen. In the extended game, Qihua won the final victory with eighteen to sixteen. The results of the four games are listed on the left.
