Local News

Celebrating Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing to Resume Leadership: Yesterday's Citizens' Rally and Parade 104

Attendance at the Rally Reached 200,000 People. All Sectors of the City Displayed Flags to Celebrate. Middle and High Schools Had a Half-Day Holiday. Airplanes Performed and Dropped Slogans. 105

Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's safe return to Nanjing, the entire city has been rejoicing. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the city's party and government organizations led citizens in holding a Shanghai Citizens' Celebration Rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing at the Nanshi Public Stadium. Over 200,000 citizens attended. After the rally, they formed ranks and paraded around the city, shouting slogans along the way. The sound of firecrackers from various shops was deafening, and the crowds of onlookers were massive, causing traffic to be cut off for six hours. At the same time, celebrations were also held separately in Pudong, Jiangwan, Wusong, and other districts. Middle and high schools had a half-day holiday. All sectors uniformly displayed flags to celebrate. The Flying Club dispatched aircraft to perform and drop slogans. In total, over one million people participated in the celebrations. The entire city was in an unprecedentedly grand state. Details are recorded below:

Venue Arrangement

The celebration rally venue was set up at the City No. 1 Public Stadium, with three main entrances and exits on Daji Road, Fangxie Road, and Dalin Road. The main stage was on the east side of the venue. A white cloth banner was hung high on the stage, with the words "Shanghai Citizens' Celebration Rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing." The Party and National flags and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen were hung in the center of the stage. Order slogans were placed on both sides. Loudspeakers were also installed on the stage, so the speeches could be heard throughout the venue. Citizens from all sectors were lined up in the field, maintaining order.

Attending Organizations

Yesterday, over 200,000 citizens from all sectors attended the rally. The atmosphere was enthusiastic and unprecedented. Participants included the City Party Headquarters, the Municipal Government and its various bureaus, the Garrison Headquarters, local associations, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, the Municipal Farmers' Association, farmers' associations from various districts, the Defense Committee, the Seamen's Union, the Security Party Headquarters, the Municipal Education Association, the Civic Training Center, the Boy Scout Council, citizens' associations from the First and Second Special Districts, the Aviation Construction Association, the Second District Party Headquarters, the Life Mutual Aid Society, the New Life Movement Promotion Association, the Municipal Fishermen's Association, the Security General Headquarters, the Labor Education Association, the Accountants' Association, the Air Defense Association, the Red Cross Society, the Pier Business Office Jushenghe Sports Association and its Nanshi branch, the Xiayi Society, the Zhiguang Society, the Sports Advancement Association, the Social Education Society, the Yongle Friendship Association, trade associations including silk and satin, rubber, knitted goods, department stores, medicinal materials, ready-made clothing, glass, firewood and charcoal, fresh pork, chilled goods, fish industry, banks, sand casting, umbrellas, coal industry, dental inlay, cigarette rolling, etc. Labor unions included Nanhua, elevator drivers, shipbuilding in the First and Fourth Districts, papermaking in the First District, civilian ship crew, winemaking, civilian shipbuilding wood industry, gengpian, cotton spinning in the Tenth District, old wood industry, wooden shoe making, sailors, cotton, ink making, car drivers, pharmaceutical industry, brief accounts, cigarette rolling in the Fourth District, medicine making in the Ninth District, aquatic wood in the First District, knitted goods in the First and Fourth Districts, cosmetics in the First District, silk reeling in the Sixth District, candle industry, tea making in the Sixth District. Universities included Daxia, Sino-French Institute of Technology, Fine Arts College, Sino-French Pharmaceutical College, Datong, Shanghai Medical College, New China, Music College, Tongde, Jinan, Soochow, China, Women's Medical College, etc. Middle schools included Minli, Zhengshi, Tongyi, Yucai, Shanghai Women's Middle School, Wuben, St. Francis, Zhirenyong, Deaf and Dumb School, Mingde, Xiaoming, China, Minguang, Dade, Peiming, Jinye, Zhaohe, Kaiming, Shangzhong, Nursery Teachers' College, Sino-French, Guohua, Peicheng, Jiangxi, Gezhi, Zhonghua, Vocational, Shengsheng, Zhengxing, Xinya, Aiqun, Junyi, Chengzhong, Shien, Minsheng Haibin, Zhengfeng, Jingye, Chengdong, Cihang, Nanyang, Xuhui, Qiaoguang, Minzhi, Minzhi, Qianye, Qingxin, Sisheng, Daozhong, Huadong, Zhonghua, Yucai, Shenmei, Nanyang Model, Huadong, etc., as well as various fellow-countrymen associations, various organizations, party headquarters of various districts, branches of various districts, totaling approximately 200,000 people.

Rally Staff

Presidium: Wu Kaixian, Wu Tiecheng (represented by Li Dachao), Yang Xiaotian (represented by Zhao Weixian), Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Tong Xingbai, Jiang Huaaisu, Huang Zhaoxiong, Zhou Xuexiang, Shi Zizhui, Li Xiangqi, Wang Jiyi, Yu Zhenhui, Wang Xiaoying, etc. Master of Ceremonies: Zhang Hanyun. Recorders: Tong Muge, Du Mengsen. Parade General Commander: Lu Jingshi. Deputy General Commanders: Huang Xianggu, Zhang Fazeng. Chief Marshal: Wang Weiming. Deputy Chief Marshal: Tao Yishan. Opening Ceremony

(1) Music was played to open the meeting at exactly 2:00 PM; (2) Singing of the Party Anthem; (3) Paying the highest respects to the National Party Flag and Sun Yat-sen's Portrait; (4) Reading Sun Yat-sen's Will; (5) Report (by Wu Kaixian, of the Presidium); (6) Speeches (by Li Dachao, Zhao Weixian, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Li Xiangqi); (7) Discussion of proposals; (8) Shouting slogans; (9) Parade; (10) Adjournment.

Chairman's Report

After the ceremony, Chairman Wu Kaixian first gave a report, stating in brief: "Today is the Shanghai Citizens' Celebration Rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Return to Nanjing. So many compatriots have participated so enthusiastically, which truly demonstrates the sincerity of our Shanghai citizens in supporting our leader. The time when Chairman Chiang was in distress in Xi'an was not long, but everyone felt indignant and depressed. On the evening of the 25th, when the news of Chairman Chiang's safe arrival in Luoyang spread, the entire city immediately erupted in firecrackers. The scene of joy and excitement can simply be described as madness. This proves our passionate desire for the leader's return. Today, our Shanghai citizens are holding celebration rallies by district to celebrate the safe return of the leader of our Chinese nation. It can also be said that we are celebrating that the Chinese nation will become more prosperous from now on, because Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is the savior of our nation. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is safe, and he will surely lead us to implement the national policies of resisting foreign aggression, saving the country, and revitalizing the nation. This is a major and profound meaning that participating citizens should understand. At the same time, we should recognize the following three points: First, after the Xi'an Incident, all compatriots were worried and anxious. From this, we can recognize that compatriots have a deep understanding of Chairman Chiang, recognizing that Chairman Chiang is our only savior and only leader. Second, although compatriots across the country were worried and anxious after the incident, they were able to remain calm as usual, which proves that our country has a sound organization and is not as scattered and flustered as in the past. Third, our leader's safe return is entirely the result of the leader's personality and prestige. This shows the greatness and brilliance of the leader's personality. Therefore, after celebrating the leader's safe return to Nanjing, we compatriots should even more support the leader and lead us to work hard in the great cause of resisting foreign aggression, saving the country, and revitalizing the nation," and so on.

Summary of Speeches

After the Chairman's report, Li Dachao, representing Mayor Wu, gave a speech, stating in brief: "Today, we celebrate Chairman Chiang's return to Nanjing with such joy. Our only leader, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, has returned safely, which can be described as joy for all people. Recalling the anxiety and indignation of the people after the Xi'an Incident, it is indescribable, and there is a world of difference compared to today's joy. This shows the citizens' expression of support for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek," and so on. Then, Zhao Weixian, representing Commander Yang, gave a speech, stating in brief: "Today, at the celebration rally for the Supreme Leader's return to Nanjing, everyone is excited and happy. How gloomy it was a dozen days ago, and how joyful it is today. This shows the people's love for Chairman Chiang. Our nation should further work hard in all aspects under the leader's leadership. This is the meaning of today's meeting. This city, as the forefront of national defense, should continue to work harder to complete the mission of revitalizing civil rights," and so on. Then, Wang Xiaolai gave a speech, stating in brief: "Supporting Chairman Chiang is the psychology of compatriots across the country. The ancient saying says, 'Adversity strengthens a nation,' which is the current situation. It is impossible to express it in peacetime, but this time Chairman Chiang suffered misfortune in Xi'an, which showed the people's enthusiasm for supporting Chairman Chiang. After Chairman Chiang issued a written statement, we can better understand Chairman Chiang's generosity, which shows that this safe return to Nanjing was also caused by sincerity," and so on. Then, Du Yuesheng gave a speech, stating in brief: "Today is the celebration rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's return to Nanjing, which expresses the citizens' enthusiasm for supporting Chairman Chiang and rejoicing. Chairman Chiang was able to return safely because of his great personality. The people of the whole country, in addition to being gratified, all support Chairman Chiang, hoping that he will continue to lead the revolution and complete the mission of revitalizing the nation," and so on. Finally, Li Xiangqi gave a speech, stating in brief: "Today, citizens of this city are holding a celebration rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's return to Nanjing. In the past two weeks, after the Xi'an Incident occurred, the people of the whole country were all saddened and indignant. The reason is that Chairman Chiang is the only leader and the only savior of the nation. Once he is in distress, it is the distress of the country and the nation. Everyone is willing to replace him with their own body. Letters and telegrams flew from all over, and many places formed welcoming and protecting groups. This kind of performance has never been seen before and cannot be resisted by any force. Therefore, Zhang Xueliang was able to realize this situation and escort Chairman Chiang back to Nanjing. Now that the Xi'an Incident has been resolved, the future great difficulties of the nation and the country will of course depend on Chairman Chiang to lead and resolve," and so on.

Passed Proposals

(1) Passed the proposal to send a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, requesting him to continue leading the revolution, thoroughly implement the national policy of resisting foreign aggression and saving the country, and revitalize the nation; (2) Passed the proposal to send a telegram to the whole country, unanimously supporting Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to continue leading the revolution, implementing the national policy of resisting foreign aggression and saving the country, and revitalizing the nation; (3) Passed the proposal to send a telegram to the Suiyuan anti-bandit soldiers, urging them to continue their efforts; (4) Passed the proposal to send a telegram of condolence to the soldiers and civilians who died in the Xi'an Incident.

Airplane Performance

During the meeting, the city's Flying Club specially dispatched two aircraft to the venue to perform aerial flight skills. They went up and down suddenly, and the citizens were greatly excited, applauding thunderously. At the same time, they scattered small red and green slogans, which were colorful and spectacular.

Parade Situation

The parade started at 2:40 PM. Each team marched in order, maintaining order. The order of the parade teams was: (1) Police Bureau patrol car team; (2) Party and National flags; (3) Large white cloth banner of the rally; (4) Police Bureau band; (5) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's portrait; (6) Police; (7) Boy Scouts and students; (8) Trained citizens; (9) Garrison Headquarters band; (10) Military police; (11) Security team; (12) Staff members of various organizations, community groups, and citizens from all sectors; (13) Defense team members; (14) Rescue team (Chinese Red Cross Society Health Bureau). Each team prepared its own white cloth banners and Party and National flags, as well as flags with celebratory slogans written on them. Each participant held a slogan or Party and National flag, with high spirits. The procession was as long as 20 li. When the vanguard returned to Heping Road and disbanded, more than half of the rear teams had not yet set off, which shows the enthusiasm and excitement of the participants. When the parade marched around the city, the crowds of onlookers along the way were massive. Shops and residents set off firecrackers loudly, and the sound echoed through the clouds. Wherever Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's portrait passed, citizens took off their hats to pay respect. The parade team shouted slogans along the way, and the audience also shouted along, which shows how deeply Chairman Chiang is loved.

(1) "Telegram of Condolence to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Requesting Him to Continue Leading the Revolution, Thoroughly Implement the National Policy of Resisting Foreign Aggression and Saving the Country, and Revitalize the Nation." Respected Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of Nanjing, Your Excellency, Your escape from danger this time, with the sun reappearing after darkness, and the news spreading, has made all people celebrate. You, sir, are the only savior of the nation. Since leading the revolution, you have worked diligently day and night, and the entire people admire you. Hereafter, we still hope that you will adhere to your inherent sincerity, follow the central government's national policy of resisting foreign aggression and eliminating traitors, lead the people, and actively strive to break through the current national crisis in the shortest possible time, thoroughly achieving the goals of saving the country and ensuring its survival, and revitalizing the nation, so as to promote national prestige and comfort the people's hopes. The telegraph expresses our deepest expectations. Respectfully, the Shanghai Citizens' Celebration Rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. (2) Telegram to the whole country, unanimously supporting Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to continue leading the revolution, implement the national policy of resisting foreign aggression and saving the country, and revitalize the nation. Please forward to compatriots across the country, all newspaper offices. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's escape from danger, with the sun reappearing after darkness, and the news spreading, has made all people rejoice. However, the Red bandits have not yet been completely suppressed, and the border bandits are still thinking of making trouble. With internal and external troubles, the national crisis is deepening. Breaking through the current national crisis still depends on Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's leadership and active struggle. From now on, compatriots across the country must absolutely support Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, follow the central government's policy of stabilizing the country internally and resisting foreign aggression externally, and continue to lead the revolution in order to complete the great cause of resisting foreign aggression, saving the country, and revitalizing the nation. We hereby send this telegram, hoping for unanimous support. It would be fortunate for the Party and the country. Respectfully, the Shanghai Citizens' Celebration Rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. (3) "Telegram of Condolence to the Suiyuan Anti-Bandit Soldiers, Urging Them to Continue Their Efforts." (Omitted above) The generals and soldiers, for the survival of the country and the life of the nation, have bravely fought with their flesh and blood, recovering Bailingmiao in one fell swoop and Damaozi in another. Their great achievements are recorded in history. At this time when the three armies are fighting with their lives and enduring the cold on the snow-covered ground, Zhang Yang's two units suddenly rebelled, seizing the commander and committing treason, speaking for the enemy bandits, reducing the country's strength in resisting foreign aggression and suppressing bandits, and causing a major blow to the nation's revitalization. Fortunately, our generals and soldiers at the front understand the great righteousness and are not moved by the absurd arguments of the rebels. They are not disturbed by the commander's misfortune. They have always remained calm and continued to work hard according to the central government's established national policy of resisting the enemy and defending against foreign aggression, so that the enemy cannot take advantage of the opportunity. This shows the generals' and soldiers' loyalty to the Party and the country, their support for the leader, and their perseverance in the face of hardship and danger. The people of the whole country are deeply gratified. Now that Chairman Chiang's sincerity has moved people and the chief culprits have repented, he has safely escaped and returned to Nanjing to continue presiding over the Party and the country's major plans. After the melee, when the generals and soldiers hear this good news, they will surely rejoice and be even more brave to deal with the enemy bandits. We eagerly await the news of victory. In the enthusiastic atmosphere of joy and commendation, the conference unanimously resolved to telegraph an award to the generals and soldiers, and prayed that under the leadership of the central government, they would quickly quell the bandit rebellion and recover the lost territory. The people in the rear will naturally provide continuous assistance to fulfill their national duty. We respectfully report this. Respectfully, the Shanghai Citizens' Celebration Rally for Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. (4) Telegram of Condolence to the Soldiers and Civilians Who Died in the Xi'an Incident. To the families of the soldiers and civilians who died in Xi'an, Zhang Yang's two units, when unification had just been completed and the whole country was united and striving to resist foreign aggression and suppress bandits, suddenly lost their minds and acted recklessly, committing treason and seizing the commander, making reckless claims. After two weeks, the central government rectified discipline and issued a clear order to punish them. The people of the whole country also rose up in response, issuing telegrams denouncing them. As a result, justice was greatly promoted and the rebels were terrified. Chairman Chiang safely escaped amid the enthusiastic cheers of the people. Since Chairman Chiang's safety is linked to the safety of the whole country, compatriots across the country, upon hearing the good news, all turned their tears into joy. However, this sudden incident resulted in countless people bravely defending Chairman Chiang and national life, fighting against the rebel army, and making heroic sacrifices. As far as we know, there are Mr. Shao Yiru, a member of the Central Committee, Mr. Jiang Xiaoxian, head of the Chairman's Headquarters Guard Group, Mr. Xiao Naihua, Secretary, Mr. Ma Zhiyuan, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and the Chairman's Guards, who almost all died in the line of duty. The number of soldiers and civilians in Shaanxi who were brutally killed in this turmoil is even more than a thousand. We cannot help but express our deepest condolences to the martyrs. However, although the martyrs have sacrificed their lives, their great achievements in safeguarding the leader and loving the country are enough to shine through the ages, like the sun and the moon. The central government, remembering their past merits, will provide appropriate condolences to encourage those who come after. We hope you will restrain your grief and maintain your aspirations, and value the country. We hereby send this telegram of condolence. We hope you will consider it. Shanghai Citizens'

City Residents' Condolence Delegation Sends Telegram to Chairman Requesting a Periodic Broadcast Speech 106

The original telegram is recorded below: "Respected Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of Nanjing, Your Excellency, with the joyful news spreading that Your Excellency has safely arrived in Nanjing, all places are rejoicing. We humbly believe that Your Excellency is connected to the safety of the whole country, and your daily life is of great concern to all people. Danish Minister to China and Siam, Mr. Oussoren, Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Afternoon After Vacation, Will Go to Beijing to Meet Foreign Minister Zhang, Expresses Pleasure at Commander-in-Chief Chiang's Safe Return 107

Mr. Oussoren, the Danish Minister to China and Siam, returned to China to resume his post after a vacation in his home country since March of this spring. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 12:00 noon aboard the Italian ship "Conte Verde," accompanied by his wife and daughter. He will go to Beijing within a few days.

The ship docked at the China Merchants North Station Wharf on East Broadway Road. Zhou Jue and Zhang Mengling, the Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Hill, the Charge d'Affaires and Consul-General of Denmark in Shanghai, Mr. Miciel, and many Danish residents went to the wharf to welcome them. Minister Oussoren exchanged brief greetings with the welcoming party before disembarking and was driven directly to his official residence on Hongqiao Road to rest. He is scheduled to go to Beijing within the next day or two to meet with Foreign Minister Zhang to report his return and to convey his congratulations on the safe return of Commander-in-Chief Chiang to the capital. After staying for a few days, he will return to Shanghai and does not intend to go to Peiping, as the Danish Embassy has already been moved from Peiping to Shanghai.

Oussoren's Remarks

A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met Mr. Oussoren on the ship. He first expressed his pleasure at Commander-in-Chief Chiang's safe return, saying that he heard the news of Commander-in-Chief Chiang's safe arrival in Luoyang when the ship was passing through Hong Kong. His previous anxiety was relieved, and he felt extremely happy. He then spoke of his concurrent post as Minister to Siam and that he had first stayed in Bangkok for three weeks before coming to China, then went to Singapore to meet his wife and others to come to China on the same ship. He felt deeply honored to return to your country and planned to go to Beijing in a day or two after resting in Shanghai.

Requesting to Offer Congratulations on Behalf of the Council to Commander-in-Chief Chiang. Elder Leaves Shanghai for Beijing to Meet Zhang 110

James Elder, a Western friend of Zhang Xueliang, arrived in Shanghai on the 18th from Xi'an via Beijing to handle Zhang's private affairs. It is now learned that Elder, since the Xi'an Incident has been resolved and Zhang has arrived in Beijing to await punishment, took the 11:00 PM express train the night before last to leave Shanghai for Beijing to meet Zhang. He will return to Shanghai in a few days.

Kawagoe Scheduled to Return to Shanghai 111

Japanese Ambassador to China Kawagoe hurriedly entered Beijing after Commander-in-Chief Chiang was in distress in Xi'an to meet with Acting Premier Kong and Foreign Minister Zhang to express concern for the safety of Commander-in-Chief Chiang. According to the information department of the Japanese Embassy, Ambassador Kawagoe congratulated the central authorities after Commander-in-Chief Chiang was out of danger. Now, due to pending official duties in Shanghai, he is scheduled to return to Shanghai from Beijing on the 30th at 8:00 AM by express train with Counselor Shimizu and others, arriving at the North Station at 2:00 PM that afternoon.

Newly Appointed Embassy Secretary Giuste Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 112

Count Giuste del Giardino, the newly appointed secretary of the Italian Embassy in China, arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 12:00 noon aboard the Italian ship "Conte Verde" to take up his post. Italian Ambassador Aloisi, Embassy Counselor Bonarelli, and others went to the ship to welcome him.

Postal, Telegraphic, and Remittance Services Between Shanghai and Shaanxi Resume After the Xi'an Incident, Parcel and Heavy Item Services Not Yet Accepted 113

According to the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, the landline between Shanghai, Xi'an, and Lanzhou has now been repaired. Telegrams from Lanzhou and Xi'an to Shanghai have been received, and telegrams from Shanghai to Xi'an and Lanzhou have also been received as usual. As for wireless telegraphs, they are unobstructed and have returned to the state before the Xi'an Incident. According to news from the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, the remittance services between Shanghai and Xi'an, such as airmail remittance and telegraphic remittance, were all suspended, and the amount of postal remittance was also restricted. Now, they have completely returned to their original state, but the remittances above Tongguan have been very congested these days, whether airmail remittance, telegraphic remittance, or postal remittance.

According to the Shanghai Postal Administration, letters from Tongguan, Xi'an, Lanzhou, and other places have been received and delivered as usual. However, parcels and heavy items from Shanghai to Shaanxi have not yet been accepted. It is reported that the postal items that have been backlogged in transit will be sorted out for more than ten days before parcels from Shanghai to Shaanxi will be delivered.

Longhai Railway Resumes Passenger and Freight Trains, Efforts Made to Clear Obstructed Vehicles, Backlogged Goods Cleared, Joint Transportation Resumed 114

Since the Xi'an Incident was resolved, the Longhai Railway immediately dispatched military vehicles and made efforts to resume passenger and freight train services. Starting yesterday, passenger trains on the line have been running on schedule to Tongguan. Freight trains have been extended to Weinan. Although the tracks above Weinan have been repaired by the engineering department, the tracks are blocked by vehicles, including 50 locomotives and more than 500 carriages. Efforts are being made to move them out. Two rows of Blue Steel carriages that were destroyed (which were used by Commander-in-Chief Chiang) were destroyed at Xi'an Station and will be transported to the factory for repair immediately. More than ten employees who were killed, such as those at Xi'an and Weinan stations, will be given preferential treatment. More than 10,000 tons of freight for joint transportation to Xi'an and other places are blocked in Lianyungang. Therefore, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the railway's joint transportation services are temporarily suspended for goods to Tongguan and above until the goods in Lianyungang are cleared. The company's losses, in terms of business, are estimated to be more than 2 million yuan. The loss of property is greater than the business loss.

Radio Station of the Ministry of Communications, New Radio Station to be Completed 115

The Shanghai Broadcasting Station of the Ministry of Communications, call sign XOHO, frequency 1300, was ordered by the ministry to increase power and build a new station. Preparations are now complete and will be completed by mid-February next spring. At that time, the whole country and East Asia will be able to listen. The station has also responded to requests from listeners in various places and specially published a bi-monthly broadcasting magazine, which will be released on January 1. All sectors are welcome to send letters with two-cent postage stamps to the station at 137 Sassoon House, Shanghai.

Materials for Replacing Rails on the Hangzhou-Yushan Section Borrowed from Domestic and Foreign Loans 117

The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Council, in order to replace the heavy rails on the Yushan-Yupu section of the Hangzhou-Yushan section, will replace the original 35-pound rails with 63-pound heavy rails. The required project cost is 2.8 million yuan. After negotiating with the China Farmers Bank, the China Land Bank of Zhejiang, and other banks to borrow funds, a draft agreement has been signed, stipulating an annual interest rate of 1% and repayment in six years. China is borrowing 1.8 million, and the China Farmers Bank and the Zhejiang Land Bank are each borrowing 500,000. The entire revenue of the Hangzhou-Yushan section will be used as collateral. Jin Runquan, the representative of the banking group, traveled back and forth between Shanghai and Hangzhou to consult and negotiate, and it has now been fully successful. A formal contract will be signed immediately and funds will begin to be collected. Therefore, with the funds in place for the rail replacement project, construction is scheduled to begin on New Year's Day next year, so that it can be completed at the same time as the completion deadline of the Nanping section project in March. However, in addition to the rail replacement project cost, a huge amount of materials such as rails and sleepers are needed. According to a reporter from Shen Shi News Agency's investigation in the banking industry, the Ministry of Railways is currently conducting a material loan from the Czech Railway Material Factory, requiring about 28,000 tons, worth 6 million yuan, with an annual interest rate of 4% to 5%, also repayable in six years. It will be handled in accordance with the method of the Beijing-Jiangxi Railway borrowing 80 million from the German Otto Wolff Iron Factory. It is currently progressing smoothly and can be formally signed in the short term. Before the material loan is signed, the rail replacement materials will temporarily borrow the materials stored in the Nanping section for general use. It is planned to complete the traffic plan of the Hangyu, Yunan, and Nanping roads in March next year to facilitate transportation and enrich national income.

Income Tax to be Implemented on New Year's Day, Ministry of Finance Officially Announced Yesterday, First, Second, and Third Categories to be Implemented Simultaneously, Foreign Merchants and Civil Servants to Pay Alike 118

The implementation of income tax is imminent, and all industries have complied with the order to prepare and are studying the collection procedures. A reporter from Shen Shi News Agency has learned from the Shanghai Income Tax Office of the Ministry of Finance that the Ministry of Finance officially announced yesterday that from January 1, 1937, all income from the first category of profit-making enterprises, (A) all profit-making income from companies, commercial firms, banks, factories, or individuals with capital of more than 2,000 yuan, (B) income from profit-making enterprises jointly run by officials and merchants, and (C) income from temporary profit-making enterprises, income from the second category of salaries and remuneration, (excluding income tax from civil servants' salaries, which has been levied since October 1), income from salaries and remuneration of freelancers and others engaged in various occupations, and income from the third category of securities and deposit interest, income from interest on corporate bonds, stocks, and various deposits, will be calculated and paid according to the tax rate. All procedures will be handled in accordance with the Provisional Income Tax Regulations and their implementation rules. It is also learned that Liang Hejun, the deputy director of the office, will concurrently serve as the Shanghai preparation commissioner, and is currently consulting with various industries on the collection methods in accordance with the instructions of the Ministry of Finance. The banking and financial industries have generally been prepared. After the implementation on New Year's Day, the funds will be collected by various fund collection agencies and submitted to the Central Bank. For inland areas where there is no Central Bank branch, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, or the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau may act as agents for collection. It is also learned that the taxation of foreign merchants from various countries has also been negotiated with the relevant governments and will be implemented at the same time, which is expected to proceed smoothly. As for the government agencies employing foreign civil servants, 20% of the maximum income tax has been deducted from their salaries since October, amounting to as much as 1 million yuan per year.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation has decided to resume all routes starting today and abolish the temporary measures for previous routes. The Shaanxi-Kunming route is scheduled to send an aircraft from Xi'an at 12:00 PM today (Tuesday), passing through Chengdu and landing, and then flying from Chengdu to Kunming at 8:00 AM tomorrow (Wednesday). The Peiping-Zhengzhou route is scheduled to send an aircraft from Peiping at 7:00 AM today (Tuesday), arriving in Zhengzhou at 10:30 AM.

Banking and Financial Industries Stipulate National Calendar, Year-End Settlement Methods, Industry Associations to Hold Meetings Today and Tomorrow Respectively, Financial Industry to Use New Accounting Methods Next Year 120

The year-end closing period of the National Calendar is approaching. The banking and financial industries have stipulated the year-end settlement methods. The financial industry will reform the accounting system next year. The banking industry will hold its 11th standing committee meeting today. The details are as follows.

Banking and Financial Industries Busy with Settlement

Since the Financial Industry Association decided on the year-end closing of accounts in the National Calendar, all banks are now preparing. Member banks of the Banking Association have completed the settlement of deposits and loans in the savings and commercial departments. The settlement of the banking and financial industries has become busy these days. The financial market has announced the interbank lending rate. Because all industries are active and the market is stable, it is very stable, which is very different from previous years. For example, the interbank lending rate was still 8% yesterday.

Two Industries to Hold Meetings Today and Tomorrow Respectively

(1) The Banking Association has scheduled to hold its 11th member standing committee meeting at 4:00 PM today. In addition to reporting on the association's affairs in the second half of 1936, it will also approve the budget and final accounts, and the Guangdong Bank will join as a member, and the Jiangzhe Bank will withdraw. As for the association's affairs report, it has been mimeographed by the secretariat and will be distributed to all members at that time. (2) The Financial Industry Association's member representative standing committee meeting was originally scheduled to be held on January 2, but it has been brought forward to 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 30th. The notice has been issued yesterday.

Year-End Methods for Banking and Financial Industries

(1) The Financial Industry Association yesterday notified its member banks that, "Regarding the proposal of the 30th executive committee of the third session to extend the time for receiving and returning bills on the National Calendar's New Year's Eve, it has been resolved that the time for the industry to receive bills on December 31 of the National Calendar will be extended to 4:00 PM, and the time for returning bills will be extended to 8:00 PM. This is specially recorded and reported for your reference." (2) The business hours of various banks to the public on the National Calendar's New Year's Eve will be extended by one to two hours, and the internal business hours will continue until the accounts are cleared. (3) The bank clearing house will add one exchange of notes on the National Calendar's New Year's Eve at 5:00 PM.

Financial Industry Reforms Accounting System

The financial industry holds meetings of managers of various banks every spring, summer, autumn, and winter to study matters related to business reform. All member banks have now been notified that they will uniformly adopt new accounting methods from next year (referring to the methods of the Fuyuan Bank, which are the same as the methods of the banks). The bank notes will also be changed to the new style with the words "or bearer" added to comply with the provisions of the negotiable instruments law. Each bank will also set up an accounting director, and the detailed methods for reforming the accounting system have been notified to the member banks yesterday for compliance.

Twenty-Year-Old Child, Impersonating Zhang Fakui's Son, Steals Father's Money and Spends it Extravagantly Outside, Resides in the Cangzhou Hotel and Claims to Still Have Guards, Drives Around the City in a Car, Eats Six Dishes, and Watches a Play, Cangzhou Manager Becomes Suspicious and Reports to the Police, Investigation Reveals the Inside Story 122

Zheng Youchang, also known as Haitao and Yufen, a Cantonese person, runs the Youchang Awning Factory at No. 38, Lane 423, East Broadway Road. He has three children. His youngest son, Zheng Fayuan, is only twelve years old and is studying at the Shanghai Municipal Council's primary school. He is quite clever but likes to steal things. He had previously stolen and spent his father's money. On the 25th of this month, at half-past two in the morning, Zheng Fayuan took advantage of his parents' absence and stole his father's

A wallet containing 150 yuan in legal currency and a platinum watch of the "Ever Read" brand, with a total value of more than 300 yuan, and took it outside. At 5:45 PM, he went to Room 317 of the Cangzhou Hotel on Jingan Temple Road, wrote the name Zhang Zhongfa in the registration book, lived at No. 2 Aihua Lane, Ever Read Road, and claimed to be the son of Zhang Fakui, the Commander-in-Chief of the bandit suppression area in Fujian and Zhejiang provinces of the National Government, and said that he still had

Two guards who would come later. The hotel servants did not doubt his false identity and treated him with great courtesy. At that time, Zheng Hai also told a servant named Wang Shiyuan that his income in Shanghai was very meager and that he would help him find a good job in Hankou, and asked Wang to accompany him to play. On the morning of the 26th, at 8:00 AM, Zheng hired a taxi and went to the Guanshengyuan teahouse for breakfast, then took the original car to play in the city center. At noon, he went to the Chunjiang Restaurant for lunch. At 3:30 PM, he went to the

Golden Theater to watch a play. The cost of the taxi alone reached 12 yuan. The manager of the Cangzhou Hotel, seeing that the child had no family members with him and behaved lavishly, became suspicious and reported to the Jingan Temple Police Station by telephone. Detective Zhang Liang and a Western detective were ordered to go to the Golden Grand Theater and found Zheng Hai. They searched him and found 40 yuan in legal currency and an "Ever Read" platinum watch, and took them back to the police station for questioning about his address. At first, he claimed to live at No. 2 Aihua Lane, Ever Read Road, but after investigation, it was found that there was no door number at No. 2 Aihua Lane. The child then claimed to live in Jiangwan Park Lane

Chen Bingqian's residence. Chen's family all said that they did not know this child. Finally, Zheng Hai confessed the truth. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court and Lawyer Qian Xunjiu explained the situation, prosecuting him for theft under Articles 320 and 324, Section 2 of the Criminal Code, and said

"It has been found that the defendant Zheng Fayuan is not yet twelve years old. Today his father has come to court and requested to take him back for custody. This lawyer has no objection." When questioned, Zheng Hai confessed to stealing his father's money. Then Zheng Youchang surrendered himself and requested to take him back for custody. Judge Pan Zhenyang verified the confession and ordered Zheng Fayuan to be acquitted and handed over to his father Zheng Haitao for custody for two years and six months.

Case of Assassination of Mining Engineer Kaya-o Two Culprits Sentenced to Death, Remaining Six Sentenced to Imprisonment Each, Eight Defendants Express Dissatisfaction and Appeal 123

The case of the assassination of Japanese mining engineer Kaya-o Kōsaku involved Mao Yonghu, Wang Zhensheng, Zhao Yunhong, Jin Daoquan, and Zhu Guisheng and Chen Enming, who were preparing to continue killing Japanese people, as well as the women Wang Zai and Zhang Ma, who supplied guns and ammunition to Mao Yonghu, etc., totaling eight people. The Shanghai District Court publicly tried the case, and after the conclusion of the arguments, the sentencing was scheduled for 2:00 PM on the 28th of this month. Yesterday was the scheduled date, and the Japanese Consulate sent Chief Inspector Kuchi Yanagi Saemon from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, along with Kawashima Tsutomu from the Inspectorate of the Public Works Department, who were guided by Zhang Youji, a clerk from the Third Section of the Municipal Police Bureau, to

observe the proceedings in court. The court ordered Police Chief Zhang Shuping and Chen Xihui to supervise all the bailiffs and be on guard in the First Criminal Court. At three o'clock, Presiding Judge Cai Dingcheng, the head of the Criminal Court, along with Judges Shao Qinshi and Li Xuedeng, Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu, and Clerk Zhou Yuejuan, arrived at the court. They also notified the appointed defense attorneys Yu Chengxiu and Shi Qinghua, both lawyers, to come to court. They ordered the eight defendants to be brought to the case. The presiding judge and others stood up and read the

main text of the judgment. Mao Yonghu and Wang Zhensheng were both sentenced to death for jointly committing continuous murder, with permanent deprivation of civil rights. Zhao Yunhong was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment for assisting in murder, with ten years of deprivation of civil rights. Jin Daoquan was sentenced to thirteen years of imprisonment for assisting in and preparing for murder, with ten years of deprivation of civil rights. Zhu Guisheng and Chen Enming were each sentenced to two years of imprisonment for preparing for murder. Wang Zai was sentenced to two years of imprisonment for repeatedly transporting firearms. Zhang Ma was sentenced to

one year of imprisonment for transporting firearms. One six-round revolver, six bullets, and one cartridge case were confiscated. After the reading was finished, the presiding judge briefly announced the reasons for the judgment, stating that Mao Yonghu and Wang Zhensheng's previous confessions were consistent with the facts, and their crimes had been proven, and the circumstances were relatively serious, therefore they were sentenced to death. As for Zhao Yunhong and Jin Daoquan, the prosecutor originally charged them with inciting murder, but the court's investigation found that it could not be proven, but the circumstances of assistance, according to their confessions, were very clear, so they were reduced to

the crime of assistance. The fact that Zhu Guisheng and Chen Enming were preparing to kill other Japanese people has also been proven and cannot be denied. As for Wang Zai, she collected and transported firearms three times, and the circumstances were more serious, so she should be punished severely. Zhang Ma's crimes were relatively few, so she was sentenced to one year of imprisonment, and so on. The detailed reasons will be sent with the judgment. When asked if the defendants accepted the judgment, each defendant claimed to be dissatisfied and would appeal within ten days after receiving the judgment. They were then taken back into custody.

Rickshaw Puller Leads to Bust of Theft Case Chen Zhenhua and Wife Conspired to Commit Theft 124

Chen Zhenhua, a 24-year-old Shaoxing native residing on the front floor of No. 8 Pingjiang Lane, Lan Weiai Road, in the French Concession, lived with his wife. Chen worked as a salesman at a certain soy sauce shop. Due to business relations, he became acquainted with Tong Guohua, an Yixing woman (30 years old) residing at No. 62 Xinling Village, Caishi Road. On the night of the 27th of this month, at 11:00 PM, Chen, accompanied by his wife, planned to steal from Tong's home. He instructed his wife to wait inside Xinling Village Lane, while he entered Tong's house alone. Under the pretext of visiting, they engaged in casual conversation. As it was cold, Tong hospitably offered to make tea for the guest. Seeing Tong leave to fetch water, Chen immediately seized the opportunity and fled with Tong's overcoat, silk gauze, and cotton quilt. When Tong returned home with the water, Chen and the stolen items were gone. She inquired around and coincidentally encountered a rickshaw puller who had taken Chen home. The rickshaw puller, upon hearing the situation, volunteered, saying that he had just taken a man and a woman with packages to No. 8 Pingjiang Lane, Lan Weiai Road, and was willing to lead the way. Tong then instructed the rickshaw puller to guide her. Chen, upstairs, heard the knocking and, feeling guilty, climbed to the roof in an attempt to escape. He was spotted by one of the people who had come along, who shouted and stopped him. Chen had no choice but to come down from the roof and return to the house. Tong also followed in, and the stolen goods were clearly in sight. She immediately reported to the French Concession police, who sent Detective Kang Yutian to take Chen and the stolen goods to the police station. Yesterday, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Special Second District, where Judge Chen Shuoying interrogated them. Police Department lawyer Chen Ming presented the case, requesting a postponement for further investigation and then prosecution. Then, the plaintiff stated the process of the defendant coming to visit and stealing. The defendant confessed without denial. The court ordered the case to be reheard on the 31st, and the defendant was remanded in custody.

Fire at Great Western Road Kills Girl 125

At the home of Yan Zai, No. 33 Yongqing Lane, Great Western Road in western Shanghai, a fire suddenly broke out at 3:30 PM yesterday. It quickly spread to the neighboring No. 34. The Caojiadu Fire Brigade, upon hearing the alarm, drove to the scene and extinguished the fire. Two houses were burned down, and it was reported that Yan Zai's daughter, Erbao, who was only three years old, was unable to be rescued in time and perished in the fire.

Hydrographic Office Determines Five Submerged Reefs Southwest of Qimu Island in Bohai Bay and Enters Them Into Hydrographic Charts 127

The Shanghai Hydrographic Office issued Notice No. 300 yesterday, stating the determination of submerged reef positions southwest of Qimu Island in Bohai Bay, and explanations for the marked position of suspected reefs on charts. (1) The position of five submerged reefs was determined: Position (A) is 205 degrees from the Qimu Island lighthouse, a distance of 12.3 nautical miles, i.e., 120 degrees 7 minutes East longitude, and 37 degrees 30 minutes North latitude, depth 12 feet (3.66 meters). Explanation: An isolated sharp reef, which should be marked on the chart with a danger line encompassing "Two Toise Stone" (each toise equals six feet). Position (B) 216.5 degrees, distance 15.2 nautical miles, (C) 216 degrees, distance 15.4 nautical miles, each with a depth of 18 feet (5.49 meters) from the Qimu lighthouse. Explanation: The above (B) and (C) are rocky slopes forming a reef, each should be marked with "Three Toise Stone," and enclosed with a danger line. Position (D) 211.5 degrees from the Qimu Island lighthouse, distance 15.15 nautical miles, depth 12 feet (3.66 meters). Explanation: An isolated sharp reef, which should be marked on the chart with a danger line encompassing "Two Toise Stone." Position (E) 205.75 degrees from the Qimu Island lighthouse, distance 14.8 nautical miles, depth 12 feet (3.66 meters). Explanation: This is a rocky slope extending northward from the shore, which should be marked with "Two Toise Stone" in the above position, and enclosed with a danger line connected to the shore. (2) Explanation of suspected reef positions marked on charts: Position (F) 219.5 degrees from the Qimu lighthouse, distance 20.8 nautical miles. Explanation: The above position is marked on the chart as "Two Toise Suspected Reef." After exploration, it was not found. Related charts are British Navy Hydrographic Charts No. 1255 and 1256. Original reporting agency: Hydrographic Office, Navy Department.

Yi'an Steamer Collides with Pier and is Damaged 136

The Yi'an steamer, managed by the Fu'an Steamer Company in this city, which originally sailed the Xinghua Quanzhou route, has now changed to the Huangyan Wenzhou route. This time, the ship was berthed at Pier No. 14 in Nanshi, Shanghai. After loading cargo and passengers on Sunday, it set sail and left Shanghai for Wenzhou. It was unexpected that when the ship was unmoored and the anchor was raised, the tide was rising and the current was very rapid. The Yi'an steamer was pressed by the rapid current, and the hull rushed towards the pier, and its port side slammed into Pier No. 14, causing four iron plates of the hull to be dented and severely damaged. Part of the pier was also damaged. After the accident, both parties sent personnel to conduct an inspection together, and at the same time reported to the company, and transferred the report to the insurance company. The Yi'an steamer can still sail and set sail as usual, and it must come to Shanghai for inspection and repair.

Commemorating the Centenary of the Famous Russian Writer Erecting a Bronze Statue in This City Location at the Intersection of Gu Gu Bi Road and Qi Qi Road 137

The Zi Lin Bao said that next February will be the 100th anniversary of the death of the great Russian writer Pushkin. This city is now preparing to hold a grand commemorative ceremony at that time to show respect. Pushkin is not only the ancestor of Russian poetry, but also the master of the Russian literary world in the 19th and early 20th centuries. The entire civilized world admires him and regards him as the most beautiful symbol given to the world by great literature. His name shines with great Russian writers such as Tolstoy, and they all admit that they have been personally influenced by Pushkin. Both within and outside the Soviet Union will hold commemorations, and in various foreign countries, there is an international situation. The Pushkin Committee in this city has been preparing for commemorative events for several months. In addition to Russian expatriates, the committee also includes Chinese, English, and French figures who admire Russian literature. The French Concession Board has agreed to allocate a piece of land for the placement of Pushkin's bronze statue. The bronze statue will be designed by Russian architects and sculptors and will be built immediately, and the unveiling ceremony is planned to be held on February 11 next year, the 100th anniversary of Pushkin's death. The location will be at the corner of Bi Xun Road and Qi Qi Road, and the place will be named Pushkin Square in the future. The commemorative program will begin on January 29 and end on February 14. On the actual day of the centenary commemoration, the French Literary Association and others will hold a meeting and invite celebrities to give speeches. One of the most noteworthy events is a grand Pushkin music concert held at the Lyceum Theatre on February 2. The best artists in this city and the music team of the Public Works Department of the Public Concession are planning to participate, and will sing Pushkin's poems and translations in Chinese, English, and French. The commemorative committee is now planning to print a booklet of commemorative programs in Chinese, Russian, English, and French, containing Pushkin's biography, comments on Pushkin by contemporary Russian writers, and more than 100 copper plates of Pushkin's portraits.

Hawkers Clash with Police in Pintang Lane, Shanxi Road Hawkers Surround Police in Serious Situation Police Open Fire in Desperation Three People Injured 138

The section of Pintang Lane, Shanxi Road, from the Nanjing Road intersection to the Tianjin Road intersection, has always been occupied by small fruit hawkers. However, the Nanjing Hotel is also located here, and traffic is frequent. However, the hawkers still gather as before, resulting in traffic obstruction between noon and evening. The Public Works Department Police Department found out about the situation and ordered the Chinese police on duty in that section to strictly ban them. However, the hawkers came back after being driven away, and they never disappeared. At about 8:00 AM yesterday, Chinese policeman No. 239 on duty in that section saw that there were more than a dozen fruit stalls resting and selling there, so he immediately stepped forward to drive them away. However, Wang Fugen, a local, 28 years old, stopped and rested his stall as before. The Chinese policeman believed that he did not obey the order and immediately arrested him. It was unexpected that Wang immediately threw the bricks used to press the stall at the policeman, resisting arrest. At this time, more than a dozen fruit vendors who had been dispersed saw it and came back together, surrounding the Chinese policeman and forcing him to release Wang. For a time, the situation was turbulent and the order was disrupted. The Chinese policeman knew that he was outnumbered, so he hurriedly blew the whistle for help. More than a dozen fruit vendors saw that the incident was escalating and immediately shouted and beat him. The Chinese policeman was in a hurry and immediately drew his gun and fired three shots, one hitting Wang Fugen's left leg, one hitting a pedestrian, Li Xigen, a Dalian native, 43 years old, in the leg, and one hitting Jiangbei female beggar Liu Xiaoqing in the leg. More than a dozen fruit vendors fled without a trace. The Laozha Police Station in charge received the report and hurriedly sent Chinese and Western detectives to investigate the truth, and also sent the Chinese policeman back to the police station for interrogation. On the one hand, they sent the three injured men and women to the hospital for treatment.

Kenye Bank in Baxianqiao Robbed by Armed Bandits Yesterday Female Bank Employees Were Petrified Doorman Shot and Seriously Injured 139

The Baxianqiao branch of the China Kenye Bank, located at No. 143 and 145 Mintiniyin Road in the French Concession, is headed by Yao Dexin, and the business department is staffed by women. The business hours are from 9:00 AM to 5:00 PM every day except for holidays. At about 4:00 PM yesterday, two bandits suddenly came, holding a pistol, jumped over the counter next to the cashier's office, and forbade them from making a sound. The female employees of the bank were all petrified. The bandits snatched 2,036 yuan in cash (including one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan subsidiary coins) placed in the rattan basket next to the desk in the cashier's office, hid it on their bodies, and jumped out of the counter. At this time, Chuan Shijun, the doorman from Beiping, saw it. He hid behind the counter on the west side and was about to draw his pistol and shoot, but the bullet jammed. The bandits saw it and carried out their plan to strike first. They held the gun and fired several shots at the guard. The guard was shot in the ribs and fell to the ground. Two holes were also shot in the wall on the west side of the bank. The bandits then went out and fled. When the robbery was being committed, the French Police Station had received the alarm and immediately sent a large number of Chinese and Western detectives in police cars to round up the bandits, but the bandits had already fled far away. They then sent the injured guard to Guangci Hospital for treatment. It was reported that the injuries were quite serious. It is said that there were a total of four bandits involved in the robbery. Two were on guard outside the door, and two entered the bank to commit the robbery. When the bandits opened fire to resist arrest, Zhang Yongnian, a Ningbo native who was an employee of Tianxiang Fashion Company on Fourth Malu, happened to be going to the bank to withdraw money. He witnessed the shooting and fled in panic. Afterwards, Chinese and Western detectives from the French Police Station went to the bank to inquire about the robbery and ordered the arrest of the bandit gang for interrogation.

Theft Cases in Hotels Occurred in Huizhong and Xinxin Respectively Two Young Thieves Have Been Detained 140

Yu Xing, the accounting director of the Haiyan County Public Security Bureau, took leave and came to Shanghai on the 25th of the month, opening a room at No. 505 Huizhong Hotel on Hankou Road. His cousin Jiang Hua was studying at Liangcai School. That evening, Yu took Jiang Hua and Jiang's female classmate Li Chen out to play at the dance hall. When they returned at 2:00 AM, they saw the window along the veranda was open. They checked their belongings and found that the jewelry, silver dollars, and overcoat placed in the room had disappeared. They immediately reported to the front desk. Next door to Yu, room No. 506, was occupied by two Western-dressed men. After Yu and others went out, the two men also went out with a woman and did not return until about 9:00 PM. They then closed the door. At about 4:00 AM, they paid the room fee and left. When the tea boy entered the room to clean up, he saw that the quilt on the bed was raised, as if someone was sleeping. He looked closely and there was no one sleeping. He lifted the quilt and found an overcoat inside, which was one of the missing items. He then determined that Yu's belongings must have been stolen by the two men who broke into the room. He reported to the police station for investigation, but there was no progress. Then, at about 5:00 AM yesterday, a similar incident occurred in room No. 513 of the Xinxin Hotel on Nanjing Road. After reporting to the Laozha Police Station, Detective Chen Shanji was ordered to go to investigate. He believed that it must have been done by the guests in the neighboring room, so he investigated. He investigated room No. 511 and saw two men in suits living inside, whose faces were the same as the guests in No. 506 Huizhong. He then arrested them and found some of the stolen goods in the room (that is, the items stolen from No. 513 Xinxin) and took them back to the police station. After questioning, the two men were identified as Cao Jihou, from Anhui, and Xu Rongqing, from Ningbo. The Huizhong tea boy confirmed that it was them without error. They were then transferred to the Second Criminal Court of the Special First District. The police lawyer Chen Ming presented the case, stating that the two men had just been arrested and had not yet been thoroughly investigated, so he requested that they be detained. He also presented records of the two men's previous theft cases. After Judge Pan interrogated them, he ordered a postponement for another hearing.

Increased Revenue for State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company During the Yangtze River's Low Water Levels; October Sees a 42% Increase Compared to Last Year 141

Since its active reorganization, the State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has diligently expanded its business, and its cargo and passenger revenue has seen rapid progress. Its cargo and passenger revenue for July increased by more than 11% compared to the same period last year, August increased by 48% compared to the same period last year, and September increased by 55% compared to the same period last year, as has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Recently, the company's business revenue for October, after settlement, was 896,148.14 yuan in national currency, compared to 630,932.47 yuan for the same month last year, an increase of 42% compared to last year. It is also reported that the company's business revenue in the previous months not only increased compared to the same months last year, but also increased month by month compared to the previous months of this year. Moreover, October was a time when the Yangtze River's water level was low and navigation encountered difficulties. The increase in its business revenue was still more robust than last year, which also shows a glimpse of the company's operating performance.

Rampant Infectious Diseases in Shanghai Port; Smallpox, Diphtheria, and Scarlet Fever are the Most Severe; High Number of Injuries and Deaths Last Week 142

Due to the scarcity of rainfall and dry climate this year, infectious diseases are quite prevalent. According to the Datong News Agency reporter's inquiry at the Harbor Quarantine Office yesterday morning, the situation is as follows:

Diphtheria and Smallpox are Severe

According to the Shanghai Port Infectious Disease Investigation Report from the Harbor Quarantine Office for last week, the number of cases of smallpox, diphtheria, and scarlet fever has suddenly increased. There were 36 Chinese patients and 6 foreign patients with smallpox, with 5 Chinese deaths and 1 foreign death. There were 30 Chinese patients with diphtheria, with 2 deaths. Scarlet fever is particularly rampant, with 24 Chinese patients and 5 foreign patients last week, and 1 Chinese death.

High Typhoid Fever Mortality Rate

The number of cases of other infectious diseases is less than last month. There were 4 Chinese patients and 1 foreign patient with bacillary dysentery last week, with 1 Chinese death. Although the number of typhoid fever patients has decreased, the mortality rate is quite high. There were 16 Chinese patients last week, with 10 deaths. There was also 1 foreign patient who died from the disease. There was 1 foreign patient with amoebic dysentery who died. In total, 105 Chinese and 13 foreigners suffered from infectious diseases, with 21 Chinese deaths and 3 foreign deaths.

The Zhonghua Guohuo Yangsan Factory, founded by Li Chunhua, located at No. 6 Jiru Lane, Jixiang Street, French Concession, is a three-story building. The third floor was used as a warehouse. This morning (the 29th) at 0:29 AM, a fire suddenly broke out in the warehouse on the third floor. At that time, the smoke was billowing and the fire was extremely fierce. The fire brigade was notified and rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire. The fire was finally extinguished at 1:40 AM. The three-story building was almost completely burned. A maid, Wenying, who was 14 or 15 years old, was sleeping in the room and died from smoke and fire. The fire brigade transported her to Guangci Hospital. It is reported that the factory had fire insurance. The factory owner, Li Chunhua, was not at home when the fire broke out.

New Economical Clothing from Tong Feng Yong Clothing Store 150

Tong Feng Yong Clothing Company, located at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Fourth Malu, is an old Western clothing store in this city with more than 20 years of history, specializing in fashionable European and American men's and women's overcoats, new-style Western clothing, raincoats, etc. Mr. Sun, the owner of the store, recently hired a Russian technician to guide the sewing. In order to eliminate the bad habit of haggling in slippery stores, he advocated the principle of small profits and quick sales. In mid-December, a large number of materials were shipped from Europe and the United States. In consideration of social economy, a new type of economical clothing was launched. For example, a new style of plaid flannel-lined leather collar overcoat is only sold for 13.5 yuan, a plain-colored flannel fox fur collar overcoat is 16.5 yuan each, and a twill flannel overcoat with a wooden raccoon fur collar is 19.8 yuan. Each piece earns only three or four corners in addition to the cost. It is completely different from those on the market who sing about great sacrifices and great bargains. Ladies from all walks of life may wish to try it to know that the words are not misleading.

Notice from the Rickshaw Industry Association to All Rickshaw Owners: The Abolition of the Non-Redemption Group Magnet Badge if Not Redeemed 156

In the rickshaw industry of this city, there has long been a dark side of stealing rickshaws and extorting ransoms, which has aggravated the suffering of rickshaw pullers. Since the establishment of the Rickshaw Industry Association's non-redemption group in May of last year, rickshaw owners have voluntarily paid 5 cents per vehicle per month to punish rickshaw thieves, transfer vagrants to labor camps, and compensate for all losses after rickshaw theft. For more than a year now, although no less than 200 rickshaws have been stolen in the north and south of the city, the majority of them have been compensated with rubber accessories by the group, and only a small number have been fully compensated with new rickshaws. When a rickshaw puller's rickshaw is stolen, they are liable for a maximum of six yuan and a minimum of three yuan, which is a great benefit to the average rickshaw puller compared to the fifteen or sixteen yuan extorted in the past. Recently, the Municipal Public Works Bureau believes that such organizations are limited to the south of Shanghai and Zhabei, and intends to uniformly implement this measure for all rickshaws in the Shanghai West Special Zone, which will be undertaken by insurance companies. After several consultations, the trend is already emerging, and it is expected to be established soon. However, the non-redemption group magnet badge nailed to the back of each rickshaw is considered no longer necessary to exist. A special order was issued to the Rickshaw Industry Association to abolish it. The association believes that since the new organization has not yet been established, the impact will be significant if it is abolished suddenly. It therefore requested a postponement of implementation and separately notified all rickshaw owners to inform all rickshaw pullers to comply with the police instructions for the abolition to avoid causing misunderstandings. Currently, many rickshaw owners have voluntarily abolished it, awaiting the authorities' proper handling of the aftermath to prevent rickshaw thieves from making a comeback.

Fire at Sanmin Palace Ballroom; Western Manager Dies Violently; Westerner Suffers Wounds and Death is Strange; Five Suspects Arrested and Sent to the General Bureau 157

Romanian Saiming, the owner of the Sanmin Palace Ballroom at the intersection of Beichuan Road and Qiujiang Road in Zhabei, was 77 years old. Around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, Saiming was working in the manager's office when a fire suddenly broke out. It was extinguished by the staff, and only documents and other objects were destroyed, with no other losses. However, Saiming was found dead on the ground, with two wounds on his head caused by a weapon, and blood flowing straight down, which was extremely strange. The Beisichuan Road Police Station in charge of the district dispatched police to investigate upon receiving the report. Five Westerners and Chinese suspected of being involved in the ballroom were detained for a brief interrogation and sent to the General Bureau. Huang Hua, the chief of the third section, questioned the case at around 10:00 AM yesterday morning. Due to the strange circumstances, he personally went to the scene to investigate and took many fingerprint photographs to begin investigating the perpetrator.

Arrest of Counterfeit Money Criminal Leads to Implication of Middle School Student; Qian Sanduo Becomes Ill from Fear; Trial Concluded Yesterday Pending Sentencing 158

In Huajing Township, Shanghai County, there is a young man named Qian Sanduo, who is a student at Nanyang Middle School. On the first day of this month, while congratulating a classmate on their wedding, he passed through Caojia Bridge in Xixiang. It happened that Sun Qiulin, who lived in Changqiao Township, was using counterfeit Farmer Bank banknotes there. Policeman Tan Shaoyun arrested Sun and also detained Qian Sanduo, who was taken to the County Public Security Bureau and transferred to the local court. Qian Sanduo became ill from fear and was released on bail by his family. Sun was detained. Prosecutor Li filed a public prosecution. The case was tried by Judge Zhang yesterday. Qian Sanduo was not present due to illness, but Sun Qiulin confessed that he had found 38 banknotes at Caojia Bridge. He said that he went to buy cigarettes and was told that they were fake, but he did not know Qian Sanduo. Witness Tan Shaoyun said, "I was patrolling in Caoxing Town and saw 20 fake banknotes on the ground. Sun Qiulin was running in front, so I arrested him. I also recovered 18 banknotes from the river. Qian Sanduo was walking in front, so I arrested him as well, but no fake banknotes were found in his pocket." At this point, the official adjourned the debate and announced that the verdict would be announced on the 31st.

Page 13 161

Commercial News

Special Feature: Production, Sales and Manufacturing of Keemun Black Tea (Continued from the 26th) 162

Keemun black tea is a high-grade tea, often fetching double the price of ordinary black tea. Its excellent quality, though expensive, is favored by Westerners. In particular, the British people are most fond of Keemun. Domestic consumption of Keemun tea is very low; almost all of the annual production is exported. In the past, Britain accounted for over 50% of the total export volume, followed by France and Germany, and then by countries such as the Soviet Union and the Netherlands. According to the export statistics of our bureau's tea inspection, the situation of Keemun exports to various countries in the past four years is listed in the table below:

The export volume of Keemun tea varies from month to month. The new tea is generally available on the market in mid-May, and Keemun exports are most prosperous in June. The amount of Keemun exported in June each year often reaches around 7,000 metric tons. After July, it gradually decreases. The following table shows the export trends for each month:

Monthly Export Volume of Keemun Black Tea in the Past Four Years (Unit: Metric Tons)

The above three tables have a common point that readers should pay attention to: the actual export volume of Keemun tea may not be as high as indicated. Occasionally, exporting foreign firms mix a small amount of other black tea into Keemun tea to enhance its reputation. However, since Keemun tea is still the main component, it is difficult to call it other tea. Therefore, this is specially noted to dispel doubts.

Keemun tea is one of our country's export teas. In addition to Keemun, other exported black teas include Hunan and Hubei's "Hu Hong" (Hubei Black), Jiangxi's Ning Hong (Ningzhou Black) from counties like Xiushui, Zhejiang's Wen Hong (Wenzhou Black) from areas around Yongjia, and Fujian's Fu Hong (Fujian Black). The position of Keemun's export volume among all exported black teas is worthy of research.

Percentage of Keemun Tea in Total Exported Black Tea

From the table above, the export volume of Keemun tea only accounts for about 20% of the total tea volume, which is less than that of other lower-grade black teas. In terms of value, there are no separate statistics for the export value of Keemun tea. However, since Keemun is of superior quality and high price, its value is naturally more expensive. Therefore, it can be asserted that the percentage of its value in the export of black tea is higher than the percentage of its quantity.

The world's tea-producing countries export approximately 800 million pounds of black tea annually, equivalent to 3.6 million metric tons. Keemun exports about 20,000 metric tons annually, accounting for only 6/1000th of the total. It can be seen that Keemun's position is very weak. Our countrymen are accustomed to the name of Keemun, but they do not know that the production and sales of Keemun are not comparable to Indian or Ceylon black tea. In comparison, it is like a small witch seeing a great one. Our countrymen should be aware of this. However, the future of Keemun tea still has ample room for development.

(3) Reasons for Fluctuations in Keemun Black Tea Market Prices

Keemun black tea has a small output and excellent quality. It has always been favored by people in countries such as Britain and the United States, so the price is very high. Domestic sales are very small, and it is mainly for export. Therefore, the market price of Keemun tea is affected by the supply and demand of black tea in the world on one hand, and it also changes due to foreign exchange rates on the other. As a result, tea prices fluctuate up and down. In particular, the market price of Keemun tea is extremely volatile, sometimes high and sometimes low, making it difficult to grasp. Fortunately, since the government implemented the legal tender policy last November, foreign exchange rates have stabilized, and tea prices are no longer in danger of sudden highs and lows. Tea merchants will also not suffer unexpected losses. The exchange rate problem has been solved, and tea prices can be stabilized, but the reality is not so. Although tea prices vary greatly due to differences in quality, the same batch of tea, of the same quality, often has very different prices due to the timing of transactions and different supply and demand conditions. This is especially true for Keemun tea, where the market price on the opening day of the new tea can differ by dozens of yuan from the market price on the second day. Therefore, the risk of operating tea is very high. Timely transportation and sales can bring double or even several times the profit; conversely, it can lead to bankruptcy. Because of this, tea prices increase, tea firms spring up like mushrooms to take advantage of it, and when tea prices fall, tea merchants struggle to survive. The main reason is that tea prices cannot be stabilized. Considering world tea consumption, black tea is the most consumed. Besides our country, the producing countries include India, Ceylon, and the Dutch East Indies. These countries have come from behind, and our country's foreign trade in black tea is just barely the fourth-largest exporter. Because we cannot control supply and demand, nor can we control the world market price of black tea, the price rises and falls according to the supply and demand of black tea in the world. If supply exceeds demand, the price falls; conversely, if demand exceeds supply, the market price rises. In summary, there are two main reasons for price fluctuations in Keemun tea: one is the changes in international black tea supply and demand, and the other is the fluctuations in exchange rates. Looking back at the situation in previous years, it becomes even clearer.

(4) Market Prices of Keemun Black Tea in the Last Ten Years

Keemun tea prices have always been very high, and the market price varies depending on the quality. The market price of high-grade Keemun tea is over 100 yuan per market catty, and sometimes even reaches over 400 yuan. The price of mid-grade Keemun tea is 70 or 80 yuan, and even the price of low-grade Keemun tea must be 40 or 50 yuan. Not only do prices fluctuate annually, but they also vary at different times within a year, depending on supply and demand conditions and exchange rates. (To be continued)
